(24th Special Dispatch)

Sichuan New Games Association Established; Chairman Chiang's Admonition; Four Points Must Be Noted to Promote New Life 9

(Chongqing) On the 23rd, Chairman Chiang attended the inauguration ceremony of the Chongqing New Life Movement Promotion Association and said that there are several points that must be noted in promoting the New Life Movement. First, to implement the New Life, one should start with the word "Li" (禮, etiquette). The so-called "Li" does not mean kowtowing three times and kneeling nine times, or bowing and raising hands, but refers to all proper attitudes, that is, all reasonable actions of self-discipline and dealing with people. As far as society and the country are concerned, it is the so-called order and discipline. Therefore, we should have "Li" at all times, in all places, and in all things. As the ancients said, "Do not speak improperly, do not move improperly, do not look improperly, do not listen improperly." We must pay special attention to the promotion of the New Life Movement and make the general public do it first. Second, the goal of the New Life Movement is to militarize, productivize, and artisticize the lives of the people. Third, in the Chinese mainland, the lifestyle, spirit, and actions of ordinary foreigners generally conform to the principles of the New Life. We should learn from their strengths and make up for our shortcomings. Fourth, in the future promotion of the New Life Movement, we should focus on leading by example, promoting the habit of labor, and the spirit of serving society. That is, the so-called "exerting their strength without leaving their bodies," and "not for oneself" in the Book of Rites, and the so-called "Everyone should aim to serve and not to take" by Mr. Sun Yat-sen. The more intelligent and capable people should use their abilities to serve hundreds of thousands of people and create happiness for hundreds of thousands of people. People with slightly less intelligence and ability should use their abilities to serve tens of hundreds of people and create happiness for tens of hundreds of people. All comrades who are determined to promote the New Life Movement should have labor service organizations. In addition to their own work, everyone should serve the society or the public for at least one hour or more. In addition, Chongqing City should pay attention to improving two things. First, there are very few cigarette advertisements in Chongqing, which is a very gratifying phenomenon, but on the other hand, there are many advertisements for panaceas and elixirs for the treatment of various dishonorable diseases, while advertisements related to academic, cultural, and educational matters are not easy to see, and the advertisements do not specify locations or pay attention to cleanliness. From this, we can see the moral and cultural decline of society and the incompetence of the police. We should know that the content and form of advertisements have a great influence on the spirit and psychology of the people. In the future, if there are advertisements that do not comply with the regulations, it is hoped that the New Life Movement Association will cooperate with the local authorities to pay attention to suppression. (2) There are many unemployed vagrants and beggars in Chongqing. The government authorities, leaders from all walks of life, and comrades of the New Life Movement Promotion Association should work together to design, based on the principles of labor service, to persuade, organize, and train them, and make them engage in various construction undertakings. As long as the government and leaders from all walks of life cooperate fully, it will be easy to do. In short, after the establishment of the Chongqing New Life Movement Promotion Association, it is hoped that the government authorities, leaders from all walks of life, and all New Life comrades will lead by example and work together to lay the foundation for building a new Sichuan and setting an example for all parts of the country, etc. (24th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Issue of Tax Reduction on Domestic Goods Exports 14

(Nanjing) Regarding the issue of reducing or exempting export taxes on domestic goods, a certain tax official said that the total value of domestic goods exports last year was 53,521,429 yuan, which is a decrease of over 7,661,000 yuan compared with the total export value of 61,182,790 yuan in 1933. This decrease has certainly affected the industry, but last year's import surplus was also significantly reduced compared with the previous year. As for the reduction and exemption methods, they are currently being discussed and it is inconvenient to speculate. However, textile fibers have always been the highest among domestic goods exports, but last year animal and animal products were the most, totaling over 77 million yuan for the whole year, followed by yarn, silk fabrics, and knitwear, totaling over 75 million yuan, while the former exported over 11.4 million yuan in the previous year, and plummeted to over 7.4 million yuan last year, falling from the first place to the third place. This situation should of course be taken into consideration when studying the reduction and exemption. However, it is definitely not just a simple tariff issue that affects its sales. In addition, tea exports increased by over one million yuan compared with the previous year, tobacco increased by over two million yuan, raw hides, tanned hides, and leather goods decreased by over two million yuan, coarse grains decreased by over two million yuan, oil [seeds] decreased by over five million yuan, fuel increased by over one million yuan, and piece goods decreased by over 16 million yuan. The fewest exports were sugar, with only over 13,000 yuan for the whole year last year. The above increase or decrease situation should be considered in terms of which are domestic needs, which are stagnant due to foreign goods dumping, and which are not enough to compete in foreign markets due to lack of improved production. In addition, although other categories have also increased or decreased slightly, the amounts are not large. As for the plan to separately reduce or exempt, its principle should be to focus on promoting domestic products, but the size of its reduction and exemption scope must take into account the social situation, and it is not possible to predict at this time. (24th Special Dispatch)

Measures for Ending Prize-Linked Savings 28

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance has drafted a proposal for measures to end various prize-linked savings schemes. The two-item measure has been jointly approved by the Executive Yuan and handed over to the Ministry of Finance for deliberation. It is reported that the content does not adequately take into account the interests of both the savings banks and the depositors. The business of all small and medium-sized prize-linked savings banks will be wound up when the Trust Bureau of the Central Bank is established. The Central Bank Trust Bureau will take over, and all unexpired depositors of the various banks will continue to pay their savings to the respective banks in accordance with the original deposit methods, and will handle them on their behalf, together with the benefits they have earned. As for new depositors, the Trust Bureau will no longer accept them. The purpose of this measure is to protect the interests of the original depositors and to have a definite time to end. Before implementation, opinions will be exchanged with domestic and foreign savings banks before a deadline for implementation is set. (24th Dispatch)

The Ministry of Finance Corrects the Terminology for Silver Dollars 29

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance notes that the public habitually refers to silver dollars as "silver ocean." The term "ocean" originated when Mexican coins were imported. This term should be corrected. It is specifically stipulated that in the future, all notes and contracts must use "silver dollar" as the representative term, and the term "silver ocean" should no longer be used. (24th Dispatch)

Current Affairs Commentary

The Terror of the Yellow River Disaster Strikes Again 35

— Du

The Yellow River's engineering situation. Suddenly, a critical report has emerged. The Puyang Jin embankment. Largely destroyed. The Guantai blockage. Unlikely to close. And the river's water level rising day by day. The flow gradually becoming fierce. Remotely remembering the disaster victims in the Lu-Yu area. Old pains not yet recovered. New worries gather again. In the mire, the mud. Fear and trepidation. The feeling of grief. Need not be deeply discussed. Now is just the beginning of spring. Yet it already presents a surging trend. In a blink of an eye, a great overflow will arrive. Breaching the dikes and changing course. Invading Wei and seizing Huai. Not only will Hebei lose its protection. But Jiangsu and Anhui will also suffer. Therefore, the fact of river defense. Is the most serious and urgent problem at present. The people of the whole country. Should be as the hands and feet protecting the head and eyes. United in mind and strength. Swiftly and promptly to go forth.

Water management work. Has always been regarded as difficult to achieve. Only by effective supervision. Can a slight effect of treating the symptoms be achieved. During the Qing Dynasty. The Yellow River breached its banks thirty-nine times. Since the overflow in Zhengzhou in the thirteenth year of Guangxu. For decades, it has been relatively calm. Just when stability and control of the river were anticipated. Who would have thought that one breach the year before last. Would again cause a major disaster. At that time, the disaster area covered. Five provinces and reached. Fifty counties. The disaster area was. As large as more than 15,000 square miles. The disaster victims numbered four million. The time lasted eight months. It cannot be said to be a great and overflowing inundation. Afterwards, although the flood period passed. The blockage project. Has not progressed. The disaster victims' pleas. Are reported incessantly. Finally, there was the breach in Changyuan last autumn. And the suffering in Hua County. Since then, the Yellow River. The terror of the disaster is deeply rooted. People's hearts and the engineering situation are dangerous. It is often felt to be difficult. At the beginning of the ice flood. It has become a serious situation. Although it is a natural disaster. Is it not also a failure of human planning?

We have also anxiously pondered. To find the crux of the problem. To say that the authorities are indifferent to the river management project. The government has set up various levels of water conservancy agencies to manage it. The organization is grand. Those belonging to the central government. Are the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission. The North China Water Conservancy Commission. Those belonging to the local government. Are the Yellow River River Affairs Bureaus of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan provinces. When the water disaster broke out the year before last. A Yellow River Disaster Relief Committee was specially established to supervise it. And its integration into the National Economic Commission. Its measures cannot be said to be not detailed. To say that the authorities have no solution to the river management. The Executive Yuan did discuss prevention and blockage. First, the six-province flood control conference decided on the steps later. And the Shandong Provincial River Affairs Bureau's proposed plan to repair and dredge the Yellow River estuary and. The outline for Yellow River management proposed by Li Yizhi, chairman of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission. Are all insightful. Orderly and organized. The government has not been without solutions. However, it has ultimately not helped the overflow of the water. To see this tense situation again. What is the reason? We are not clever. Dare to cover it in one sentence and say. Although there are many agencies, no one is truly responsible. Although there are methods. But those below do not implement them vigorously. Precisely because no one is responsible. Criticisms are numerous. Fittingly increasing excuses for shifting blame. Precisely because they are not implemented vigorously. Documents fly about. Only seeing empty words. Last year, the disaster victims in western Shandong sent a telegram appealing for the blockage of the breach. It was said. "Personally went to the mouth to check. Although the dry mouth is closed. The water mouth has not yet moved. Even if there is equipment. The work is not at all tense." Li Yizhi also said after inspecting the river work. "The river works in the three provinces have not used new methods. The follow-up projects are particularly sloppy." And the supervisory committee member Zhou Lisheng's report after being dispatched to investigate the situation of the Changyuan breach. Even directly said "The old dikes are not solid at all. Afterwards, when the disaster occurred. The protection was not vigorous." These are all indications of the facts. There is something that is difficult to conceal.

At this time today. With the dangerous situation in front of us. We truly do not need to look for the gaps of the past. To make pointless resistance. Only by gathering the strength of everyone can we jointly. Quell the great disaster. Looking at the opinions of certain important members of the Jinghui. It seems that the non-identity of powers and responsibilities has also been seen. And the Tianjin telegram came. It said that the new engineering office has been established. Kong Xiangrong and Li Yizhi are responsible for blocking the breach and cultivating the dikes. A unified command will be seen. Old malpractices will be corrected. And a new era will be ushered in. Hanging up the overturned cart to warn future generations. This is what is hoped for from the efforts of all the gentlemen.

A sudden explosion at an arsenal in the southern suburbs of Harbin - The city shook, order was disrupted, bullets flew, followed by a massive fire - The cause is unknown and remains under investigation 36

(Harbin) This question concerns the arsenal in the southeastern suburbs, which exploded at 11:00 AM this morning, shaking the entire city. The number of deaths and injuries is unknown, but the dead must number at least dozens, with even more injured. Many nearby houses were burnt down. Within a mile, all glass windows were shattered. Bullets flew everywhere, and residents were terrified. As of 6:00 PM this evening, the sounds of explosions had not completely subsided. Only one ammunition depot has not yet been affected, but it is feared that it will not be spared in the end. Military authorities have dispatched troops to surround the arsenal and prevent people from approaching. Manchu and Japanese soldiers are making every effort to put out the fire, but have failed to extinguish it. (24th Reuters Dispatch)

(Harbin) At 10:55 AM today, the arsenal of the Chinese Eastern Railway guard troops in Majiagou, between the Japanese barracks and the airfield south of the city, suddenly exploded several times. All the cannons, large and small, and shells, etc., in the arsenal were completely destroyed. Nearby residents fled to other places. Japanese aircraft inspected the state of the explosion from the air. The sounds of explosions subsided at 12:10 AM, but five or six large warehouses of the nearby Chinese Eastern Railway guard troops were burned down. The explosive sounds shocked the entire city of Harbin. The ammunition depot of the army and navy, 200 meters away, was also on alert for an explosion. In addition, the nearby troops have all been concentrated in Harbin to take charge of security in the city. On the other hand, the large glass windows of the Tonglun Foreign Firm in New City Street, one and a half miles away, were also shattered by the explosive sounds, resulting in great losses. As for the cause of the explosion, it is currently under investigation. Also, the fire was extinguished at 1:00 PM. Residents who had fled to other places have also returned to their homes, and order has been restored. (24th Dentu Dispatch)

(Harbin) When the arsenal of the Chinese Eastern Railway guard troops exploded, many of the glass windows and doors of shops in the Majiagou area were shattered. Those who took refuge flocked to New City Street, creating a tragic scene inside and outside Harbin. Fortunately, no people or animals were injured. However, two guards have already fled. The sounds of explosions ceased at 1:00 PM, and people's hearts have also returned to calm. The cause of the explosion is currently unknown, and the losses are also difficult to estimate. (24th Dentu Dispatch)

After the Illegal Sale of the Eastern Route, Japan Plans to Resolve the Outstanding Issues Between Russia and Japan, Starting with the Fishing Treaty and Oil Rights. Ota Will Return to Russia Next Month to Negotiate. The Russian Far East Minister Departs Japan for Home 37

(Tokyo) After the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Foreign Minister Hirota plans to resolve all outstanding issues between Russia and Japan. (Tokyo) Foreign Minister Hirota answered the following questions on the North Pacific Fisheries Control Law Committee in the House of Representatives on the 24th regarding the revision of the Japan-Soviet fisheries treaty and the purchase of North Sakhalin Island:

(1) The Soviet Union operates North Pacific fisheries as a state-run enterprise, adopting complete control and management. Therefore, Japan must also focus on protecting national interests and confront it. It is still appropriate to organize a large-scale fisheries company to control it. If a unified agency for fisheries companies is established, I feel that Japan will have an advantage in the negotiations on revising the Japan-Soviet fisheries treaty, and it will be profitable. As for the ruble issue that has become an outstanding issue, although it has not reached a final resolution, it may be possible to conclude it at the time of revising the treaty. It is not yet known whether the Soviet Union still intends to sell it as before, but I sincerely hope that this period will come. As for the trial digging of oil mines and the exploitation of forests, etc., I hope that the activities of Japan in the economy will not cause diplomatic obstacles. (24th Japan United Press Dispatch)

Changes to the Eastern Route Train Schedule

(Shenyang) After the Chinese Eastern Railway is taken over, the every-other-day round trip between Harbin and Manzhouli and between Harbin and Suifenhe will be changed to once a day, but the train between Harbin and Suifenhe will still run during the day. Establishment of a Price Arbitration Committee

(Tokyo) The Chinese Eastern Railway Transfer Agreement was officially signed on the 23rd, and at the same time, the first installment of 23.3 million yuan in cash was paid. About two-thirds of the total price of the road is in the form of material payments, and the total amount will be paid off in the next three years. When implementing it, when there is disagreement between "Manchuria" and the Soviet Union regarding the determination of the price of goods, the price arbitration ruling committee selected by Japan, "Manchuria," and the Soviet Union will obstruct the discussion and exercise the decision. Yesterday, when the agreement was signed, the decision of the arbitration committee was discussed as a matter for later discussion. Now, after consultations between Japan, "Manchuria," and the Soviet Union, the general situation has been decided as follows on the 24th: (1) The Price Arbitration Ruling Committee will be located in Tokyo. (2) The Japanese side's committee member has decided to appoint Mr. Kurisu, the director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Trade Bureau. The "Manchukuo" side's committee member is Mr. Hoshino, the director of the Ministry of Finance (but in practice, the administrative officer Mr. Ito will be his agent). The Soviet side's committee members are Mr. Laichter, the counselor of the Soviet Embassy in Japan, and Mr. Zelezhnijakov, the first secretary of the embassy. (24th Japan United Press)

A Russian Newspaper Publishes an Article to Comfort Itself

(Moscow) The Soviet government's gazette, Izvestia, has an article entitled "The Consolidation of Peace in the Far East," discussing the official signing of the Chinese Eastern Railway sales agreement. It said: "This move, whether viewed from the perspective of general development or from the current situation in the Far East, is an important political event. The Chinese Eastern Railway was once a tool for Tsarist Russian imperialism to carry out its aggressive policies in the Far East. At that time, it helped to divide China. The relationship of the Russian masses to this policy was only that they had to use their own labor to make this tool for implementing imperialist policies, and at the same time, they had to sacrifice their blood for the results of this policy. Later, the proletariat overthrew the Tsarist Russian regime and eliminated the rule of the bourgeoisie, but it could not simply abandon the Chinese Eastern Railway empty-handed, because a large amount of national funds had been invested in the road. Not only that, but the proletariat had striven to prevent the road from collapsing, so that it would not be affected by the warlord melee, and then transferred it to the Chinese people, so that the road would become a tool for the two major countries to practice friendship. Although the last point was impossible to achieve, until today, China has still failed to get rid of the shackles of foreign imperialism. Because of the setbacks of the Chinese masses, China has become increasingly weak. Therefore, Manchuria has separated from China, and foreign troops have controlled Chinese territory. As a result, armed conflicts have occurred. This kind of conflict is most intense near the railway. If the business of the Chinese Eastern Railway is not protected by strong military force, it cannot be carried out peacefully. Since the Soviet Union has resolutely abandoned the Tsarist Russian era's territorial expansion and colonial plundering policy, it can never maintain the business of the Chinese Eastern Railway by force, because if force is used, it is tantamount to participating in the imperialist division of Manchuria. There is already a 'regime' in Manchuria. In order to preserve the people's investment in the road as much as possible, and in order to avoid conflicts (this kind of conflict often occurs around the Chinese Eastern Railway and at the same time threatens peace), the Soviet Union deems it necessary to sell the Chinese Eastern Railway to this 'regime.'"

"The enemies of the Soviet Union and the Chinese people have said that this matter shows the Soviet Union's setbacks in the Far East," and they want to use this to alienate the nationals of the Soviet Union and China. The enemies of the Soviet Union hope that the Chinese Eastern Railway dispute will cause a war, but the Soviet Union's peace policy and its strong strength have shattered this hope, forcing those who love to plunder to abandon their idea of solving the Chinese Eastern Railway problem without an agreement. Now there are some people who think that since the Chinese Eastern Railway problem has not caused a war, they should at least use its peaceful solution to alienate the Chinese nationals from the Soviet Union, but this move will also be in vain. Chinese patriots with brains will be able to see through that if this road can be transferred to the representatives of the great Chinese nation, then what pleasure would the Soviet Union not have? The Soviet Union's broad masses of people cherish the friendship of the Chinese nationals extremely. Unfortunately, the Chinese nation is no longer the master of Manchuria. Once the road becomes a target of contention, and this important Far East transportation route is destroyed in one fell swoop, then what benefit will it have? The Soviet government insists on avoiding conflicts in the Far East no matter what, because this is not only to maintain the Soviet Union's national defense or Soviet interests. The Chinese Eastern Railway sales agreement was then announced successfully. Izvestia said, "We hope that the Japanese government can fulfill all its obligations and faithfully fulfill the signed agreement. This point is of great benefit to the consolidation of Soviet-Japanese relations. There are still several disputes between the Soviet Union and Japan. Their resolution must be conducted through serious negotiations with the spirit of mutual concession, understanding, and concern for the promotion of peace between the two nations. If these kinds of negotiations are to have meaning and can have satisfactory results, then the Japanese government must express its willingness to fulfill the agreement every day when implementing the Chinese Eastern Railway agreement. Today, 'The European side is putting peace to a serious test. The Far East can now untie a knot of dispute, which is doubly joyful, because the Far East is the center of the greatest war crisis. The Soviet Union's policy combines the firm effort to strive for peace with the belief that maintaining peace requires a force worthy of respect, so it can complete this task. The Soviet people should welcome this decision on the Chinese Eastern Railway, because it is a factor in promoting peace in the Far East. They hope that the Soviet Union will be able to achieve this goal in all places where peace is threatened in its continued struggle to maintain peace." (24th TASS Dispatch)

Results of the Paris Conference: British, French, and Italian Positions Converge; Berlin Talks Based on London Declaration; Further Discussions in Northern Italy After Return of British Cabinet Members from Eastern Tour 40

(London) After a sincere exchange of views in Paris yesterday among the representatives of Britain, France, and Italy regarding German rearmament, doubts were dispelled and harmony restored. The British Lord Privy Seal, Eden, the French Foreign Minister, Laval, and the Italian Undersecretary of State for Foreign Affairs, Suvich, met at the French Foreign Ministry from 1:20 AM to 5:10 PM yesterday, with only a short break for lunch. The result was complete agreement. Before the meeting adjourned, it was decided to hold a further conference on April 11 in Stresa, on Lake Maggiore in northern Italy. According to sources in Rome, the Italian government warmly welcomes inviting Germany to participate, as the Italian government's policy of advocating a four-power compromise is not new. British, French, and Italian circles have all expressed satisfaction with the outcome of yesterday's talks in Paris. The French and Italian sides now sympathize with Foreign Secretary Simon and Eden's visit to Berlin, and Eden's subsequent visits to Moscow, Warsaw, and Prague. London is particularly pleased. The characteristic of yesterday's talks in Paris was that France and Italy consistently supported Britain's position. (Reuters, 24th)

Official Communiqué Issued

(Paris) The following communiqué was issued after the meeting:

"The French Foreign Minister, Laval, the British Lord Privy Seal, Eden, and the Italian Undersecretary of State for Foreign Affairs, Suvich, met today at the French Foreign Ministry to exchange views on the general situation. During the talks, it was reiterated that the visit of the British cabinet members to Berlin was of an exploratory nature, and that the scope and objectives of the British-German talks would be based entirely on the provisions of the London Declaration of February 3. The governments of Britain, France, and Italy hold a unified opinion on this matter. The talks also decided that, after the British cabinet members have visited Germany and continued their visits to the Soviet Union, Poland, and Czechoslovakia (all of which are supported by the French and Italian governments), the foreign ministers of Britain, France, and Italy should hold a meeting in Stresa, Italy, on April 11. Laval, Eden, and Suvich expressed great satisfaction with the complete unity of contact among the three governments. (Havas, 23rd)

France and Italy Express Satisfaction

(Paris) The talks between Britain, France, and Italy today ended at 5:10 PM. Political figures are deeply satisfied with the communiqué issued after the meeting, which stated that the three governments are in agreement. It is generally believed that today's talks gave French Foreign Minister Laval an opportunity to reiterate France's position on German rearmament, namely, that Germany's current rebuilding of its army not only gives Germany the military equality it demands, but also makes the German army larger than those of its neighbors. Therefore, in future talks, France cannot recognize this decision by Germany.

Rome Italian newspapers commented favorably on the outcome of yesterday's trilateral talks in Paris, stating that the Rome Agreement of January 7 and the London Agreement of February 3 had already demonstrated the unity of views of Britain, France, and Italy. The Paris Conference reaffirmed this, and therefore the conference is sufficient to establish a strong foundation for future negotiations and is of great spiritual importance. (Havas, 24th)

Collective Security System

The Anglo-French declaration of February 3 solemnly stated that Germany would only be allowed to change its military system if Europe obtained a collective security system. France still advocates concluding mutual assistance pacts in Eastern and Central Europe to seek collective security. Laval also mentioned this during today's talks.

No Mention of Economic Sanctions

Although news reports said that the possibility of economic sanctions against Germany was discussed at today's trilateral meeting, this was not actually mentioned. The most important future development in European diplomacy will be the visit of British Foreign Secretary Simon to Berlin. Simon's visit to Berlin will be exploratory in nature, and its outcome will not be binding on France and Italy. After Eden has visited Russia, Poland, and Czechoslovakia, the British and French foreign ministers will jointly travel to Stresa, Italy, to hold a trilateral meeting with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. The extraordinary meeting of the Council of the League of Nations may be held after the Stresa meeting. (Havas, 23rd)

German Conscription Law to Be Promulgated Imminently 41

(Berlin) The government will promulgate a conscription law tomorrow to implement the compulsory military service system announced on March 16. This law was originally intended to be published as soon as possible, but it was likely delayed until now because British Foreign Secretary Simon was about to visit Germany, and it was not appropriate to rush the matter before his visit was confirmed. Some newspapers say that the government intends to discuss this issue with Foreign Secretary Simon, and therefore to publish this law. The method of implementing compulsory military service can be glimpsed from the writings of several military experts. Major Weigelt, a member of the Ministry of Defense, recently published an article explaining the educational significance of conscription, saying that German soldiers want to inject new elements into the life of the Third Reich. Captain Wedel, another member of the Ministry of Defense, said that the new military organization is based on the principles of the imperial era. Citizens from the age of eighteen to forty-five should be conscripted. Those aged nineteen to twenty-one are assigned to the regular army, those aged twenty-one to thirty-five are assigned to the reserve army, and those aged thirty-five to forty-five are assigned to the auxiliary reserve army. The current quota for the regular army is as high as 300,000 men, but due to financial constraints, it may not be possible to conscript all of them, and their training will be completed in other ways. On this point, General Metzsch believes that military training can be carried out in the Nazi Party's military academies, middle schools, and primary schools. He said, "Primary school teachers should be assistants to military training officers. We must make the maximum effort in military affairs." It is noted that the training provided by the German Labor Service Organization is actually no different from military training. (Havas, 24th)

Italian Military Mobilization Aimed at Defense 42

(Rome) News today indicates that Italy is prepared to immediately recall six classes of soldiers. If recalled, Prime Minister Mussolini will have a large army of 1.5 million men under his command. In addition, there are 400,000 Fascist troops who can be mobilized immediately if necessary. According to informed sources in the capital, Mussolini does not want to disrupt peace, but only wants to defend Italy and resist any foreign aggression. Therefore, he has ordered all Italian soldiers to be prepared to be dispatched at any time. (National Telegram, 24th)

(Rome) The Italian government is successively dispatching reserve soldiers from the 1911 to 1914 classes to the military. By April 15, the actual strength of the Italian army will be 560,000 men. The Italian government considers this measure to be a precautionary measure. According to Prime Minister Mussolini, "Italy must have adequate defenses so that Italy will be fearless in the face of any developments." In addition, Italy is paying close attention to the situation in Central Europe after German rearmament. Italy believes that since Germany has abolished the military clauses of the peace treaty, Hungary, Austria, and Bulgaria should do the same. It is also heard that Hungary may restore compulsory conscription before the upcoming elections. (Havas, 23rd)

(Geneva) The mobilization of reserve soldiers of the 1911 class by the Italian government is viewed by international figures here as purely a precautionary measure, even more so than the mobilization of troops due to the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. (Havas, 23rd)

(Rome) After Italian Prime Minister Mussolini issued an order yesterday to call up the 1911 class of conscripts and delivered a passionate speech at the Blackshirt rally, the Italian people were extremely excited. US Seaplane: Non-Stop Flight Sets New Record; 17 Hours, Over 2,000 Miles 48

Miami, USA The 19-ton "Oriental Flying Boat" seaplane today set a new world record for long-distance non-stop flight. US Senate: Passes Work Relief Bill; Silver Amendment Also Passed 49

Final Vote in Both Houses May Be Overturned

(Washington) Today, the Senate, following the House, passed President Roosevelt's $4,880,000,000 work relief bill by a vote of 66 to 16. This is the largest appropriation ever passed by both houses of Congress. Before the bill was passed, the Senate also passed the Democratic Senator Thomas's proposed amendment to the Silver Act, stipulating the following four articles: (1) The Treasury Department is ordered to issue silver certificates, using existing silver bars and silver purchased thereafter at a price of $1.29 per ounce as collateral. These silver certificates will be used to pay off maturing debts, so that they can circulate in the market. (2) After the Treasury Department receives these certificates, it should add the words "reissued" and continue to circulate them in the market. (3) (4) The Treasury Department is authorized to issue silver certificates at will, using silver obtained from selling gold to other countries, and silver paid by other countries to settle debts owed to the United States at a negotiated price as collateral. Although the Silver Amendment is now included in the original bill, it is expected that it will be deleted during the conference between the two houses. It is estimated that the currency expansion required by the Thomas Amendment will reach $375,000,000. (Reuters, 23rd)

President Roosevelt Approves Philippine Constitution; Autonomous Government Established in November; Full Independence After Ten Years; Constitution States Respect for US Sovereignty; Murphy Busy Refining Economic Relations Between the Two Sides 50

(Washington) President Roosevelt has recently approved the Philippine Constitution. Those present included the Speaker of the Philippine Senate, Quezon (who may become the first President of the Philippines), the Speaker of the Philippine Constitutional Convention, Recto, and the current Governor-General of the Philippines, Murphy. The new Philippine government will be formally established in Manila in November of this year. The Philippine Constitution is entirely based on the US Constitution, stipulating that there will be a President and Vice President, each serving a term of six years. The Congress will only have a Senate, with 120 senators. There will also be a Supreme Court, with 11 justices. The Constitution states that war will not be used as an instrument of national policy. According to the law passed by the Philippine Congress, the Philippines should gain full independence within ten years. (Havas, 23rd)

(Washington) President Roosevelt has approved the Philippine Constitution today, and the Philippines can immediately hold elections to establish a semi-autonomous government. The constitution is largely based on the Tydings-McDuffie Act. Today's signing by the President took place in the White House Cabinet Room. Those present included Philippine and American leaders such as Governor Murphy, Senate Speaker Quezon, Constitutional Convention Chairman Recto, Senator Tydings, Secretary of State Hull, and Secretary of War Dern. After the President's approval, he sent the nomination of Riffle to be a Justice of the Philippine Supreme Court to the Senate. The Philippine representatives then issued a statement thanking the President, saying, "This move further consolidates our confidence in the US government and increases our gratitude to the American people." The constitution states respect for US sovereignty and stipulates a bicameral legislature with senators serving six-year terms and representatives serving three-year terms. The current governor appointed by the US President will be replaced by a popularly elected president, serving a six-year term and not being eligible for reelection. The judicial system will be similar to the current system, with judges appointed by the President and approved by the Senate. The rights of the people are similar to the US Constitution. The issue of women's suffrage will need to be discussed by the National Assembly in the future, and can only be passed if more than 300,000 women vote in favor. The marriage system is based on equality between men and women, and freedom of religious belief is complete. (National Telegram, 23rd)

(Washington) President Roosevelt has approved the constitution of the Philippine Islands today, allowing the Philippines to propose a republic ten years later. However, judging from the situation after today's ceremony, the final separation between the Philippines and the United States may have to be delayed. Many Philippine officials and American officials who are concerned about the Philippine independence struggle attended today's ceremony. After praising the constitution, President Roosevelt handed the approval document to Philippine Governor Murphy. Murphy then congratulated Philippine Senate Speaker Quezon, who is expected to be the first president of the Philippine autonomous government. The autonomous government will be established on November 15 of this year. Secretary of War Dern was also present at today's ceremony. Murphy will serve as the first US envoy to the Philippine Islands. He will now convene a special meeting of the Philippine legislature to decide on the date for holding a plebiscite to pass the constitution. According to the Philippines' new status, it will no longer enjoy the current free trade rights between the United States and the Philippines. Therefore, Murphy has been busy in recent days refining the economic relationship between the US and the Philippines. Murphy is currently afraid that if the United States suddenly erects tariff barriers against the Philippines, the new Philippine government will not be able to survive. Therefore, Murphy and Quezon are eager to establish a preferential mutual relationship between the US and the Philippines to preserve the current strong trade between the US and the Philippines. Quezon and his comrades are also very busy preparing for the start of a new democratic government in the East. The legislature will invite personnel from the US government, business community, and press, and invite foreign governments to send envoys to Manila in November of this year to participate in the ceremony for the establishment of the new government. After President Roosevelt approved the Philippine Constitution today, he said that he would appoint Philippine official Recto as President of the Philippine Supreme Court to reward him for his work as Chairman of the Drafting Committee. He also said, "The constitution that the Philippine Constitutional Committee presented to me is in line with the provisions of the Independence Act. I am very happy that the members have worked hard and completed a task that is vital to the life of their nation, which is worthy of celebration. The American and Philippine peoples, motivated by feelings of harmony, sympathy, and loyalty, are engaged in a great experiment. During the era of the autonomous government, this experiment will continue until the United States finally gives up its sovereignty over the Philippines and the Philippines gains complete independence." Then, the Philippine delegation and the staff members of the Philippine Office in the United States, Teldado and Guavara, all said that the Philippine people are extremely grateful to President Roosevelt for his generous approval of their constitution. President Roosevelt approved the constitution shortly after it was submitted, which is even more proof of President Roosevelt's generosity and attention to the happiness and freedom of the Filipino people. They also said that President Roosevelt's actions have strengthened our trust in the United States and increased our obligations to the United States. The Philippine Constitution stipulates the Philippine republican system and recognizes US sovereignty. Philippine officials swear allegiance to the United States. Risto's appointment as President of the Supreme Court is to fill the vacancy left by American official Street, who will resign on May 1. (Reuters, 23rd)

Hungarian Bishop Criticizes Government 51

Polish New Constitution: Majority Vote Passes House; Gives President Dictatorial Powers; Prime Minister Responsible to President 52

Warsaw The Polish constitution was established on March 17, 1921. On May 12, 1926, the current Minister of Military Affairs, General Piłsudski, staged a coup d'état, and a new constitution was created to strengthen government power. This new constitution was recently passed by the House of Representatives by a vote of 260 to 135. Members of the National Democratic Party, the Christian Social Party, the Socialist Party, and the Communist Party all voted against it. The Ukrainian Party and the Jewish Party abstained. The German Party did not participate in the discussion. (Havas, 24th)

Warsaw The characteristic of the new constitution passed by the House of Representatives today is that it expands the power of the President. The President is the Marshal of the Army and can decide to make peace and declare war. He appoints the Prime Minister, and the Prime Minister is responsible to the President, not to the House of Representatives. The House of Representatives may request the removal of the cabinet or cabinet members, but the motion for removal should be passed by both houses of Congress. The President may issue certain documents without the countersignature of the Prime Minister. When the House of Representatives declares dissolution, the President may promulgate substitute legal orders, but not to change the constitution. The Senate election law still maintains the principle of selecting outstanding people. Two-thirds of its members should be elected by both houses of Congress from among citizens with outstanding achievements. The remaining one-third should be appointed by the President. Members of the House of Representatives should be elected by direct, general, proportional election law. Their term of office is five years. They have the right to initiate legislation and pass budgets. The government also has the right to initiate legislation. This new constitution does not take effect immediately, and it is not yet decided when it will take effect. As long as Minister of Military Affairs Piłsudski continues to hold supreme power, this new constitution is not of great importance. (Havas, 24th)

The Saar After Voting to Return to Germany (French Correspondence) 70

Soaring Prices, Increased Unemployment, French Border Heavily Guarded

On January 13th, the Saar people voted in a general election, and 90 percent (528,704 people) voted in favor of returning to the Fatherland, Germany. It has been more than a month now, and in two weeks, the Saar will change to a new environment. Before the vote was implemented, everyone was very excited and happy, thinking that light would come soon. In the atmosphere of patriotic enthusiasm and high-profile propaganda, they couldn't wait to return to the Fatherland, Germany.

The general election movement that had been waiting for fifteen years has passed. After the extreme excitement of the general residents, workers, small businessmen, farmers, etc., the Hitler government calculated an unprecedented victory. In fact, "Germanism" is just a coat worn by the National Socialist Party. Apart from this coat, how much of the true spirit of Germany is there? However, the swastika emblem is displayed everywhere, which is a new scene. The "everything" of the Saar local social system has been changed by the National Socialist Party. The former political organizations and commercial organizations have all been suspended or reorganized. For example, the Catholic Youth League, the Sports League, the Socialist Club, etc., have all been called "illegal organizations" and banned. This is exactly the dream that the minority faction pointed out during the vote about returning to the Fatherland. At least many people feel that life is inconvenient and not as good as they originally hoped.

After March 1st, the League of Nations Administration Committee was removed, followed by the withdrawal of international troops and the guards of the People's Voting Committee. The Saar will soon be peacefully handed over to Germany. The conflict between Germany and France may be reduced as a result. However, on the other hand, the French mobile units and customs offices, which had not been fortified between France and the Saar before, were all prepared before March 1st and were about to establish very strong defenses. All places where the Saar borders France immediately became the strict German-French border. On the surface, it still seems to maintain a calm attitude, but the Nancy and other fortress areas—extending from the Swiss border to Luxembourg—have built very solid steel defense positions or concrete fortifications. Those places are distributed with French guards, carrying guns and ammunition, staring at the actions of the other party, and constantly reviewing and practicing, as if the enemy is coming. Although France does not have to send troops to the left bank of the Rhine, it is at least a little nervous about Germany and is doing its best to guard against Germany. Since the League of Nations decided to return the Saar to Germany, there has been a huge economic change in the Saar region, starting with the food hoarding movement. The market price of meat has also risen sharply. Other daily necessities, such as wool and cotton fabrics, canned goods, and kerosene, are all at high prices. These things will soon be as expensive as on the German border, rising by an average of 40 to 50 percent because the Saar did not levy such heavy taxes before. After being returned to Germany, they must pay the same tax rate as Germany. For example, American cigarettes such as "Lucky" and "Chesterfield" could be bought for only three francs in the Saar, but they cost six and six francs in France, and thirty francs in Germany when converted into francs. After returning to Germany, the general cost of living will naturally increase.

Before 1929, the Saar also had unemployment problems. At that time, the monthly average was only more than 3,870 people. Now it is different. At the beginning of January this year, there were 33,594 people receiving unemployment insurance. In the past, Saar coal miners could transfer to France, but now the number of unemployed people in France has also exceeded 400,000, and the Saar has become German territory again. France will further restrict Saar workers from crossing the border, and the Saar's unemployed workers will naturally become more and more difficult.

The Saar is a place that produces coal, with an annual output of 12 million tons. In the past, about 40% was sold to France, 40% was consumed by the Saar itself, 8% was sold to Germany, and the rest was exported to other countries. In the next five years, France will need 2.2 million tons of Saar coal every year. If it does not increase its purchases, the Saar's only industry will experience operational difficulties. (February 19th, Paris)

Liaoji: Volunteer Army's Resistance Against the Enemy Approaches Crisis 71

Puppet County Magistrate of Tonghua Shot and Killed by Volunteer Army; Volunteer Army Leader of Dongfeng County Arrested; Acheng County Under Heavy Siege by Volunteer Army

Northwest Inspection Notes 72

— Special Correspondent of This Newspaper, Geng Ya

Promising Prospects for Animal Husbandry in Gansu

Xie Biwen, the magistrate of Anxi County, hired workers to build the Confucian Temple in preparation for a primary school site. Due to the county's financial difficulties, half of the required materials were donated by the people. At the same time, the county government also sent workers to build the Anxi Airport on the Mud New Route. The project is quite large, and the people are working hard to do it. The person in charge of the airport is a German named Bao Ke. Because he likes hunting, he rarely goes to the airport to guide. The workers have no experience in this area, especially the farmers who come from two or three stations away. They are hungry and cold and eager to complete the work. They often fill the depressions too high and are ordered to dig them down again, which wastes a lot of the people's energy. It is said that Magistrate Xie is also planning to build a new primary school site and jointly plan a junior high school outside the pass with Dunyu counties. This matter is originally an important plan for cultural development. The rural economy outside the pass is already on the verge of collapse, and the existing primary schools are struggling to maintain themselves.

Regarding the shooting case in Xingxing Gorge that was heard on the way to Xinjiang, the Anxi garrison has captured three bandits, and one leader has escaped. After interrogation, it was learned that the bandits were all from Linxia, Gansu. The county was the ancient seat of Qinghe Prefecture, Bao'an, and was garrisoned by a general. Han and Hui people live together, and the people are known for their strength and courage. In particular, Datong Township is the source of repeated rebellions. The land in Hongtu Mountain in the township is barren and difficult to cultivate. The residents have difficulty making a living, so they first take risks, and then it becomes a common practice. The bandits' attire is like that of wealthy merchants. When they encounter travelers, they pretend to be friendly and kill them unexpectedly. If they are arrested by the government, they have often agreed in advance that someone will be responsible for a certain crime, and that person will step forward and admit it, without implicating others. If the government's trial is not appropriate, it is feared that it will lead to a major change. Past precedents are numerous, and even now there is a children's rhyme that says, "It is hateful that the people of Dongxiang have rebellious hearts from generation to generation. They are treacherous and deceitful and harm the people of the entire county." The people of Long often say that the fame of Datong Township in Hezhou is almost no less than that of Yangliuqing in Tianjin, but the reasons for the fame are different. Since the former Qing Dynasty, most of the county magistrates assigned to the county have been selected for their ability, which shows how difficult it is to govern. However, temporary dignitaries have emerged, which is unmatched by other counties. For example, former Gansu Chairman Ma Fuxiang, Ningxia Chairman Ma Hongbin, Qinghai Chairman Ma Qi, Xinjiang Chairman Jin

Page 8

Shuren, and the current Ning Chairman Ma Hongkui and Qing Chairman Ma Lin, are all from Linxia. To have six provincial chairmen from one county is rare in the country. In addition, the military officers of all levels in the two provinces of Ning and Qing, and the garrison in Hexi, Gansu, are mostly from Linxia, accounting for 70 to 80 percent. It is said that people in Liling County, Hunan Province, obtained more than 2,000 belts for military merits after the Northern Expedition. It is estimated that Linxia's belts can be comparable.

Lanzhou ice pears and Guanzhong cantaloupe are famous winter fruits. Eating them can relieve coal poisoning. Ice pears are small and easy to eat, while ice melons are large and firm, heavy as stone mortars. When you use force to cut them open, the core is all ice, bright as pearls and jade, which is very beautiful. When you chew them, they make a sound like broken jade, which is more interesting than eating ice cream. It is a pity that there are no such delicacies in summer. Returning east by car from Anxi, the rivers passed by have frozen solid. The wheels travel on them as if on flat ground. Sometimes the ice cracks and the wheels sink, and rescue is very difficult. Also, when the wheel axle touches water, it freezes and cannot turn as soon as it is blown by a cold wind. It can only be driven after being burned with coal gas. In winter, the ground springs in the villages in the Anxi South Mountains freeze, and the ground and houses are raised high. After the spring thaw, the frozen ground suddenly collapses, which is easy to be shaken down. The extreme cold outside the Great Wall is so great.

When the garrisons outside the Great Wall change defenses, the towns and cities they pass through all hang red cloth high to show welcome. I once asked a shopkeeper, "Why don't you write words on it?" He replied, "Today is the farewell committee, and tomorrow is the welcome army. If we write them all down, where will we get so much cloth?" Although this is the economics of people changing due to poverty, it can also be seen that there is a grand scene of officials coming and going in the remote border areas. When I stayed at his store, I saw "donation flyers" pasted on the wall, as numerous as snowflakes. It was the temporary fee for the whole village to welcome the army that day. Each household was assigned a certain amount of money, and the "donation flyers" had also been sent. They were newly pasted on the wall. In addition, the "donation flyers" for grain taxes and corvée are too numerous to count, especially the "assign a sheepskin," "assign ten pounds of camel hair," and "assign a student" flyers, which are rare in other places. Then I asked, "What will happen if those who are assigned are unable to pay?" He replied, "Then it is inevitable that the county police will whip and bind them. There is a song in the village that says, 'The county police go to the countryside, as vicious as tigers. Give them ▢▢ ▢, they want sheep, sleep on a hot kang, and also want a wife. If they are not satisfied, they will be tied up and whipped'—these are all true. As for sheepskins, camel hair, opium, etc., they are all transferred to the army. Students are assigned because they cannot afford to study." Hearing this, one can imagine the harshness of miscellaneous taxes.

The annual output of Yumen Shishan is 40,000 to 50,000 catties, and each 100 catties is worth more than three yuan. The mine owner has six shares, including four full shares and four half shares, for a total of eight families. The annual sales of cash or exchanges for cloth are divided equally according to the six shares. The capital of each share was 400 strings of cash when it was opened during the Qing Tongzhi period. By the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, someone had mortgaged half a share for 600 yuan, which shows that the profit was not small. The oil is purely made by local methods. The oil springs emerge from the ground. They are scooped up and placed in wooden barrels. Holes are drilled in the bottom of the barrels. Due to the specific gravity, the spring water leaks down, and then you get the rock oil. The composition of the oil is excellent for chemical experiments. It is said that the government once planned to use new methods for mining, but it has not yet been realized.

Gansu was the land of six counties in ancient times, with fertile fields for thousands of miles, lush water and grass, and animal husbandry was known to the world. For example, West Lake in Anxi, Tuchengzi in Yumen, Daxiaohonggou in Shiyansi, as well as Yemachuan in Zhangye, Shouyang Mountain in Longxi, Maxian Mountain in Lintao, Mawu in Minxian, Zhuoni in Lintan, Chengmali in Zhangxian, Chiuniu Slope in Nanshan, Guanshan in Longde, Northeast Township in Qingyang, Bailaozi in Guyuan, Qingshuizui, Sujiabao, Qingshui Ditch, Malian in Wenxian, Wangtang Erba, Cao Mei Mountain, Xiadan Fort, etc., are all natural large pastures with lush water and grass. During the Qing Guangxu period, eight major horse farms were opened in Caohu, Jiuquan, and each ranch in Gansu and Liang had as many as three or four thousand horses. After the Republic of China, the horses in Ganzhou still belonged to the government's pastures. In the twelfth year, a branch factory was established in Haiyuan, and more than 600 horses were distributed from Gansu. The Maxian Mountain in Lintao also established a horse ranch at the same time. The breeding and reproduction of each factory was robust, and the results were remarkable. Later, affected by the war, the factories were abandoned one after another, and the official property was sold at a uniform price. Animal husbandry is only a sideline of farming, and it is not easy to see herds of hundreds or thousands of horses, cattle, sheep, and camels in various places. It is clear that it is declining day by day. Now, the committee has sent personnel to investigate animal husbandry in Gansu and Qinghai, and is also establishing a Gansu-Qinghai livestock improvement experimental farm. They will first select breeds of cattle and sheep, and study the source of diseases. It is hoped that the association will be able to promote it effectively and universally revitalize animal husbandry in various places, so that the lush water and grass and rich resources of Gansu Province will not be abandoned like a wasteland for a long time.

Tianjin Yarn Industry Bankrupts: All Affected by Dumping of Japanese Yarn 73

Tianjin Correspondence: The Tianjin yarn spinning industry has been affected by the dumping of Japanese yarn and the high price of cotton and low price of yarn. During the past year, it has been struggling in hardship every day. The decline in business is more than the year before. There are six factories in the city: Yuyuan, Yuda, Huaxin, Baocheng, Beiyang, and Shenyuan. Yuda is operated by the Japanese on behalf of their creditors and is actually a Japanese-owned factory. Its business relies on special relationships and is beyond the reach of the general public. Baocheng Hengyuan stopped work one after another last autumn due to deficits. The workers were laid off. Only three factories, Yuyuan, Huaxin, and Beiyang, continued to produce finished products and did not stop work. Before the past year, Beiyang was reorganized into Xinji Company due to debts and taken over by someone else. Yuyuan has accumulated more than 5 million in arrears over the years, and its debts exceed the total amount of assets. The Japanese creditors even proposed to manage the factory and collect debts. So, it also implemented a shutdown in the name of liquidation. Therefore, among the six major yarn factories in Tianjin, excluding Yuda, which is operated by the Japanese, only Huaxin is fully operational. Beiyang's real estate industry is not optimistic. Fixed assets, including land, buildings, machinery, furniture, and parts, are estimated at 9,039,000 yuan according to the book. After deducting depreciation of 1,872,000 yuan over the years, the book value is 7,166,000 yuan. However, after detailed estimation by various accountants, the value is no more than 5 million yuan. Over the past ten years, the factory has owed a total of 5,176,000 yuan in Chinese, Japanese, and foreign debts, and some unsettled interest is not included. Last year, the factory reduced its work efficiency due to sluggish yarn sales, only operating at 70% capacity, producing an average of 5,000 bales of yarn per day, including various coarse and fine yarns. The average selling price of each bale of yarn was 192 yuan, including labor and materials, but it lost about 10 yuan. The more it produced, the more it lost. If the factory shuts down, the creditors will rush in, the workers will lose their jobs, and the severance pay and meal expenses will be endless. As a result, the factory suffers even greater losses, so it has to grit its teeth and continue to operate. However, it stopped work before the past year and originally planned to resume work last month. Later, the shareholders held repeated meetings to discuss that with so much debt, if it is not liquidated and continues to operate in a lifeless manner, the difference between capital and debt will become greater and greater in the future, making it more difficult to repay. If it is forced to resume work now, it must raise another 1.5 million in cash, with 500,000 to first repay part of the debt, 500,000 to reorganize the machinery, and 500,000 as working capital. The shareholders do not agree to increase capital, so it was decided to lay off the workers first and elect five shareholders as liquidation committee members to carry out the liquidation first, and then discuss whether to resume work. It is estimated that the liquidation will take time and cannot be completed in a short period of time. It is not known whether the factory will shut down permanently. The Beiyang Yarn Factory originally had 30,000 spindles and 2,000 workers. Last year, due to poor business, it reduced its scope, producing only 2,000 bales per day. Before the past year, it was reorganized due to losses and was taken over by Xinji Company. The old company owed a foreign firm in Tianjin 8,000 taels, which Xinji Company was responsible for repaying. Both parties agreed to repay 1,000 taels first, and the remaining 7,000 taels after the Spring Festival. Unexpectedly, after Xinji Company took over, the recession continued, and it was unable to repay the debt on time. The foreign firm applied to the court and impounded all the furniture, machinery, and factory doors of the factory a few days ago. Later, all the workers, seeing that they had lost their jobs, petitioned the Social Bureau and the Party Department separately. After negotiations between the two agencies, only the furniture was impounded, and the factory was urged to allocate funds to repay the debt as soon as possible. Fortunately, the factory was barely able to resume work. At a time when bad news about Chinese yarn factories is frequently reported, it is said that Mitsui & Co., a Japanese trading company, plans to build a large-scale yarn factory in Balitai, Tianjin South, to replace Yuyuan and Beiyang. The matter is in the planning stage. If it is realized, the lifeline of the North China yarn industry will be entirely in the hands of foreigners. (21st)

Hunan Drought Relief Association Borrows Money from the Banking Sector 75

The Loan Amount is 2 Million Yuan; The Purpose is to Handle Disaster Relief

Changsha Correspondence: Hunan suffered a severe drought last year. Among the 70 counties in the province, the disaster-stricken area reached as many as 64 counties. There are more than 10 million disaster victims to be relieved. The Hunan Provincial Drought Relief Committee was established last year, running around and appealing for relief both inside and outside the province. As a result, only more than 600,000 yuan was raised, which has long been spent. As the spring plowing is approaching, in the disaster-stricken areas, not only has the rice price risen to 20 to 30 yuan per stone, but there is money but no market, and there are no seeds available for spring plowing, especially in the areas above Yuanling in western Hunan and above Hengzhou in southern Hunan. He Jian, Chairman of the Provincial Government, has transported the provincial bank's stored grain, the flood relief association's work loan stored grain, and the provincial warehouse's grain, totaling about 500,000 to 600,000 stones, to equalize the price, but it is just a drop in the bucket and does not help. The Drought Relief Committee members discussed again and again and decided to use the rice and salt public shares or the public assets and state-run businesses of the entire province as collateral to borrow 2 million yuan from the Changsha banking sector to rush to handle agricultural loans. If the banking sector refuses to borrow money, it will ask the banking sector to raise funds on its own to handle agricultural loans or transport grain to the disaster areas to equalize the price. This matter has been approved by the provincial government and is scheduled to be discussed with the heads of various banks at the Drought Relief Association on the 24th of this month. The proposed measures have been sent to the heads of various banks. The letter stated, "Respected Sir, Xiang Province encountered a rare drought last year. The extent of the disaster-stricken area and the severity of the disaster situation are unprecedented. Although this association has appealed in many ways, the central and local governments, as well as various provinces and ports, all feel financially difficult, or replied that they are unable to help, or used the excuse of delaying the fundraising and remittance. Therefore, after half a year of handling, the outside of the province only obtained 150,000 yuan from the Shanghai fundraising of various provinces' drought relief charity associations, 1,800 yuan from the Qingdao Two Lakes Fellow Villagers Association, and 1,600 yuan from Committee Member Xu Dong Fan. Other rice and salt public shares, disaster relief public bonds, and disaster relief tariffs have been repeatedly sent representatives to Beijing to negotiate, but they have not been realized. Within the province, only the Provincial Relief Association has allocated 250,000 yuan from the salt tax surcharge successively, and the Flood Relief Aftermath Committee has allocated 100,580 yuan from the existing emergency relief funds. The provincial government has advanced 50,000 yuan from the salary deductions of various agencies to help relief, and this association has sent a letter requesting a further allocation of 50,000 yuan to be distributed for emergency relief. The total amount of funds raised is only 609,200 yuan, which has been successively distributed for winter crop seeds and spring relief, and has been completely distributed. However, it is just a drop in the bucket, and the remedy is still not much. The resources are exhausted, and fundraising is truly lacking. As the spring plowing is approaching, and there is a shortage of both money and grain, it is a great disaster for millions of disaster victims. I believe that managing the distribution of relief funds is originally a legitimate business of the banking sector, and that lending money to help disaster relief is something that you, dear presidents, have always agreed with. In addition to sending separate letters, we have prepared several points of measures and sent them for your consideration and handling. We have also scheduled a luncheon on the 24th of this month, and we hope that you will come to the meeting to discuss everything. The attached measures are as follows: (1) Use the 7,445,000 yuan owed by the Ministry of Railways to Xiang Province as a guarantee for rice and salt public shares to borrow 2 million yuan from various banks in Changsha City, with a monthly interest rate of 8%, and the repayment period is half by the end of 1935 and the principal and interest will be fully paid by the end of 1936. The borrowed money will be distributed by this association to various disaster areas for agricultural loans, and the loan methods will be determined separately. (2) Use provincial public assets or state-run businesses as collateral to borrow 2 million yuan from the Changsha banking sector. The interest rate and repayment period, as well as the relief plan, are the same as the above item. (3) The Changsha banking sector will gather a fund of 2 million yuan and imitate the methods of the Hunan China Foreign Relief Association to independently handle agricultural loans in various disaster areas, but the monthly interest rate should not exceed 1%. The repayment period is half by the end of 1935 and the principal and interest will be fully paid by the end of 1936. (4) The Changsha banks will gather funds and freely transport grain to various disaster areas in need for sale to help the people's food." (December 22nd)

Ma Hanzhang, the Fourth District Training Commissioner of the Provincial Security Office, concurrently served as the director of the Security Corps Platoon Leader Training Institute. Jiading Bamboo Worker Commits Suicide Out of Shame and Indignation 84

Qiu Asheng, a 41-year-old bamboo worker who works north of Xueqiao Bridge on Nandajie Street in this city, has a mentally ill brother, Afu, and a younger brother, Alian, who both died of illness two years ago. Recently, due to poor business and financial difficulties, he owed a lot of money for cigarettes in the Yuelai grocery store across the street and could not pay it back for a while. At about 5:00 pm on the 23rd, he went to Yuelai again to ask for cigarettes on credit. Yuelai refused to give him credit again because the previous debts had not been paid. Asheng felt ashamed, and others humiliated him. Asheng was ashamed and angry, and went home to get his usual chopper and cut his throat to commit suicide. Suddenly, blood splattered everywhere, and he lost consciousness. People rushed to help him to Cunren Hospital for treatment. Because his esophagus was broken, he died at 7:00 pm.
