Economic Supplement

How the Banking Industry Should Respond 208

— Wang Yutong

Since the economic circles of various countries have been deeply affected by the depression, they have all sought ways to relieve and restore the situation. On the one hand, they have striven to find ways to develop externally, so that what is lost here can be compensated for by others; or they have tried to get out of the atmosphere of the depression as soon as possible. In the final analysis, all of this is nothing more than an economic policy of benefiting oneself at the expense of one's neighbors. Unfortunately, China is in the midst of this trend of economic depression. In terms of economy, it lacks the ability to protect itself, so those who are watching around are gathering their sights on us. In the past few years, China has been struggling under the dire economic conditions of successive disasters, rural bankruptcy, and the decline of urban industry and commerce. In addition, it has suffered from the economic exploitation of various countries, such as the cheap dumping of foreign goods, the oppression of Chinese factories by foreign factories in China, and recently the unreasonable auction of the Shenxin No. 7 Factory, which has become a virtual certainty. The destruction of our national industry is now even worse.

Financial capital is the greatest source of material resources for maintaining national survival. Throughout history, in addition to invading China's national industries, various countries have also launched a strong conquest of China's financial capital, which is obvious to all. Just look at the activities of foreign banks in China, which is enough to prove it. According to statistics, there are 25 foreign banks opened in Shanghai, and their power is far greater than that of Chinese banks. Recently, since the United States announced its silver policy, it has actively absorbed Chinese silver. As a result, foreign banks have transferred their silver reserves overseas, causing the Chinese financial market to suddenly experience currency contraction, triggering a credit panic, and financial turmoil has followed. Under this kind of situation, China itself is declining economically, and its industry and commerce are not prosperous. It is impossible to remedy the extraordinary situation through the adjustment of international trade. It must be that Chinese banks purchase silver from overseas and return to Shanghai, such as the recent Financial Committee ordering silver bars from London and shipping them back to replenish its reserves. There is really no other way. The foreign banks in China are planning to take the opportunity to further absorb silver: (1) Each bank is increasing the interest rate for its original depositors. This is contrary to the low-interest rate policy of absorbing deposits that foreign banks have always adopted. In the past, the deposit interest rate of foreign banks was generally only 1 or 2 li. When the war in Jiangsu and Zhejiang broke out, ignorant wealthy merchants generally changed their cash deposits to foreign banks. At that time, each bank charged a storage fee because there were too many deposits. In recent years, it is difficult to count the huge profits that each foreign bank has made by taking advantage of this abnormal phenomenon. However, since the rise in overseas silver prices in recent years, each foreign bank has had to resort to absorbing deposits in order to use Chinese silver to transport it abroad to obtain greater benefits. However, with the passage of time, China's economic situation and the economic knowledge of the people may be slightly different from the past. Therefore, they use the sweet bait of raising interest rates as an inducement tool. (2) If only raising interest rates as bait is not enough to absorb a large amount of cash, then it must rely on restoring the issuance of banknotes to complement each other. Recently, the HSBC, Mercantile Bank, Yokohama Specie Bank, and Zhengjin Bank in Shanghai, led by HSBC, have agreed to restore the banknote issuance policy. According to recent statistics, the new banknotes issued by HSBC have reached more than 10 million yuan. Other banks, such as Citibank, are also rushing to make new banknotes and preparing to issue them. The most important thing for a bank to issue banknotes is to have sufficient reserves. In the past, the reason why the banknotes issued by foreign banks won the trust of the general public was largely due to their sufficient reserve funds. Taking the statistics of January 23 as an example, HSBC Bank had 83.921 million yuan in silver reserves, Mercantile Bank had 72.469 million yuan in silver reserves, Zhengjin Bank had 20.209 million yuan in silver reserves, Taiwan Bank had 7.536 million yuan in silver reserves, and Citibank had 25.551 million yuan in silver reserves. It is estimated that the issuance of banknotes is less than 2% of the silver reserves. However, the situation this year is very different. According to the statistics of January, HSBC's silver reserves have decreased to 3.723 million yuan, Mercantile's silver reserves have decreased to 1.9 million yuan, Zhengjin's silver reserves have decreased to 3.39 million yuan, Taiwan's silver reserves have decreased to 3.688 million yuan, and Citibank's silver reserves have decreased to 8.006 million yuan. Compared with the same period last year, HSBC alone has decreased by 80.198 million yuan. It is beyond doubt that this significant decrease in reserves must be due to a large amount of exports. However, the bank's reserve funds are dwindling, and the bargaining chips are insufficient. Once an accident occurs, it will affect the bank's credit. Therefore, in order to prevent any eventuality, foreign banks are trying to restore banknotes in order to attract a huge amount of cash, which can be used to replenish reserves and can be exported again. Killing two birds with one stone, there is no better plan than this.

Today, however, our financial industry is in an unprecedentedly serious period. If we do not unite and deal with the economic invasion of foreign banks carefully, the disaster will not only destroy the monetary credit and good phenomena that our financial community has worked so hard to create over the years, but will also allow foreign banks to restore their former dominance over Chinese banks and the advantages that foreign currencies have gained in the market, which is even more dangerous. Therefore, for the sake of the future, I believe that (1) we should first adopt the bank merger policy adopted during the Japanese financial panic. Small banks with weak capital and unstable foundations should merge and reorganize with each other according to their similar natures in order to concentrate capital and unify goals, so as to consolidate the credit system. (2) Each bank should take on the responsibility of promoting domestic goods and supporting industry and commerce. The general public should absolutely trust domestic banks under the leadership of bankers in order to maintain the reputation of domestic banknotes. (3) Hiding one's illness for fear of treatment is a great taboo for people. In the past, the problem with China's financial industry was that it was self-sufficient. As the saying goes, "Sweep the snow in front of your own door and don't care about the frost on other people's roofs." Therefore, it was easily taken advantage of by foreign forces and destroyed its own defenses. In recent years, people in our industry have deeply realized the mistakes of the past and are working together to correct them. If we can pay attention to sound organization and orderly steps in the future, then the way to deal with it lies in this! March 16, 24th year, in Peiping

The Decline and Future of the Native Bank Industry 209

— Wu Xiaochen

I.

Not long ago, the native banks in Wuxing, because they owed money to the Suzhou native banks, were unable to repay it for a while, and their counterparts jointly published a notice of disassociation in the newspaper. I think everyone still knows about this unprecedented tragedy. Isn't this the beginning of the decline of the native bank industry? Originally, the Chinese native bank industry has a long history, so it also has a considerable reputation and status in society, and it is also full of deep impressions. Its mission is to regulate the financial surplus and deficiency of various industries, so it is closely related to all aspects of society, from production to consumers. Therefore, the rise and fall of the native bank industry must shift with the rise and fall of the entire social economy; it is by no means something that one person can revitalize or something that can be expanded temporarily. Everyone knows that Wuxing is the center of China's silk area, so in recent years, Chinese silk has plummeted as a result of the economic encroachment of the great powers. Wherever sericulture is popular, it will naturally suffer the most serious damage first. The native banks in Wuxing, being in the midst of it, could not withstand the blow from their Suzhou counterparts. Under their weak capabilities, they could not avoid being in a state of financial embarrassment. How could their credit to the outside world not declare bankruptcy? As a result, some collapsed, some stopped, and out of the fourteen counterparts, only one was left to continue operating in the midst of encirclement. This kind of miserable situation, although not an isolated incident, has created a serious situation, which no one can deny. Therefore, shocking news followed one after another: such as the twelve native banks in Jiaxing, in addition to successively closing down, three more went bankrupt last autumn, resulting in other banks successively suspending business. Four native banks in Haiyan were completely stranded in one year. Only one of the more than 20 native banks in Changzhou was left to support the remnants. Nine of the 18 native banks in Wuxi were left, five of the more than 30 in Zhenjiang were left, and eight of the 17 in Pinghu were left. As for the native banks in Chongde, Xiashi, Hangzhou, Changxing, Shaoxing, Qingpu, Suzhou, Danyang and other places, there has hardly been a place that has not decreased in recent years. And it is not only the silk area that is like this, but also the native banks in Tongzhou, Yangzhou, Bengbu, and even Hankou, which is the commercial center of Central China, have also suffered the same fate, with some collecting accounts, some clearing, and all falling off the stage. And the native banks in Anqing were completely shut down. In Kaifeng, the closure of the Xinchang Bank caused the industry to suffer at the same time, leading to financial turmoil. Moreover, Xinchang branches were set up in seven provinces: Shandong, Jiangsu, Hubei, Henan, Shaanxi, Hebei, and Shanxi, so the impact was even greater. After the Yijusheng Bank collapsed in Jinan, Chengdehou continued to close down, and the news spread throughout the city. In Xuzhou, the grounding of the Gongyu Bank caused the banknotes of private pawnshops to suddenly be squeezed, resulting in a storm in the financial world. In Guangzhou, the collapse of the banks continued one after another, causing people's hearts to fluctuate and banknotes to plummet. And the scene in Shantou is even more dangerous. Although the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and others have tried their best to maintain it, the stability of the market cannot be achieved by a cup of water and a load of firewood. As a result, the credit of the banks has fallen even further. After the three banks of Chen Yuanda and others, who were known as the backbone members, closed down due to the wave, the three banks of Guangfa and others followed suit. How can the situation of financial panic become more and more intense? Finally, Jiafa and Guangxingchang and other banks also announced their closure in this scene. Such a situation of following the trend can be said to be like the wind blowing grass! Recently, in Fuzhou, Tianjin, Tangshan, Peiping, and Taiyuan, the source of pawnshops, many banks have been unable to stand firm and have successively announced their closure. And Xiamen, which is in the midst of a sharp drop in real estate prices, collapsed three major native banks known for their strong capital in one week, causing the financial community to feel precarious. Even Shanghai, which is known as the best area in the country, no matter how you embellish it with gold and jade, after all, in this time of crisis everywhere, Shanghai, although prosperous, cannot be compared with the other paradise of the pastoral poet Tao Jingjie, where "the old and the young are happy and at ease." Therefore, the native banks in Shanghai cannot avoid the disaster. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, the number of banks in the north and south markets reached 87, which can be said to be a scene of thousands of atmospheres, and it was the most prosperous year since the Republic of China. Or perhaps the saying that prosperity must decline is just the time to give it its authority, so the Shanghai native banks after the 17th year of the Republic of China are like a thermometer that has no ability to resist the pressure of the cold and gradually shrinks: only 84 in the 18th year of the Republic of China, only 78 in the 19th year of the Republic of China, only 72 in the 21st year of the Republic of China, and only 68 in the 22nd year of the Republic of China. It is not said that at the end of last year, unfortunately, the financial turmoil suddenly expanded, and the four banks of Baodayu and others were sacrificed as a result; then four more were announced to be liquidated, so only 57 banks were listed this spring, compared with the 17th year of the Republic of China, it has decreased by more than one-third. In this way, the native bank industry today is shaking in the east and withering in the west. The declining scene has the same picture of a hundred holes and thousands of sores. Of course, this kind of unbearable picture is not Tang Yin's "Tiger" or Zhao Zixu's "Horse", which can be used for the entertainment of the leisure class. We should see that behind this picture, there is extremely vivid rendering: what about rural bankruptcy? Is industry and commerce dying? Is the unemployment panic serious? And the concentration of capital? And even the plummeting of prices? The stagnation of real estate, etc.? Shocking, appalling, sad and tearful scars, anyone with a heart will sigh in unison when they see it!

II.

A country has its own financial center, and a place also has its own financial center. In the past and even now, wasn't the native bank industry grasping the financial center of various places in China? Therefore, the establishment of native banks in various places is very common; perhaps because society needs this kind of financial organization very much. Moreover, under the immutable law, the standpoint of the native bank industry has always maintained the so-called ethical institutions such as taking righteousness as profit inherited from a certain era, so whether it is to people or to oneself, it is based on credit. This is the characteristic of the Chinese native bank industry, and it is also catering to the psychology of the Chinese people. Especially for the decent merchants under the traditional idea of "everyone wants face and trees want bark," they dare not take it lightly and absolutely do not want others to despise them in order to maintain their reputation, because it is related to business gains and losses, and they always take credit as a prerequisite. The native bank industry can have such conditions, so it has had the opportunity for sound development in the past.

Now? The decline of the native bank industry is an undeniable fact. The glory of the past is just a historical trace! Therefore, isn't the reason for the decline worthy of careful understanding? In the past, the growth of the native bank industry was based on the word "credit," which means "people cannot stand without credit." So, isn't the general credit contraction in the country in recent years a fatal injury that has forced the native bank industry to take the wrong path? (To be continued)

Domestic Bonds in the Last Three Years 210

— Qin Heling

Our country's industry and commerce have been hit hard by the September 18th Incident, almost to the point of collapse. Domestic bonds have also been deeply affected, with the prices of various bonds plummeting by tens of dollars. In the 21st year [1932], the January 28th Shanghai Incident occurred, the situation became serious, and the market was closed for as long as three months. The bond market lost its liquidity, the financial system became stagnant, and there was a risk of fundamental upheaval. Bondholders and the financial authorities negotiated to reorganize domestic debt, proposing measures to reduce interest rates and extend the repayment period. The securities market then reopened in May. Initially, prices were low, but because the interest earned was still around two percent per month, investors took advantage of the low prices to buy in, and the bond market rose steadily. However, due to the precarious situation and the lack of a proper resolution to the issues with Japan, and with heavy clouds in the international situation, investors hesitated, and speculators were also wary. The market sentiment was depressed, and transactions were reduced. The total transaction volume for the year was only 901,710,000 yuan, a decrease of 2,439,290,000 yuan compared to the 3,341,000,000 yuan in the 20th year [1931]; in other words, less than one-third of the volume of the 20th year. Price fluctuations were also more moderate, with the average difference between the highest and lowest discounts being 23.217%, only half of the average difference of 42.94% in the 20th year. By the 22nd year [1933], border alerts were frequent, Yuguan fell, Rehe was lost, and the flames of war were raging; however, the bond market thrived, because in recent years, the rural economy had collapsed, the inland areas were bankrupt, and cash from all over the country was concentrated in Shanghai. For a time, there was an abundance of idle capital in the city, with no avenues for investment. Everyone regarded bonds as the last resort, and the amount of negotiable securities was lacking, so prices rose accordingly. Later, the Tanggu Truce was signed, signaling a temporary end to the conflict with Japan. In addition, former Finance Minister Song's successful cotton and wheat loan in the United States greatly boosted morale, and bond prices soared. This firmness lasted for several months. In November, Song resigned and was replaced. In December, a rebellion broke out in Fujian Province, creating disturbances, and the bond market weakened. Fortunately, the Fujian rebellion was quickly suppressed, morale was good, and the slump was like a flash in the pan, and soon recovered. Trading was quite brisk that year. The total par value for the year was 3,219,955,000 yuan, an increase of 2,318,245,000 over the 21st year. The average price discount also increased by 9.13% compared to the 21st year. From January to August of the 23rd year [1934], the bond market was always under the control of the bulls, prospering and reaching its peak for a time. New high prices emerged one after another, almost every month. Although the Tibet Treasury incident caused a temporary slump, prices rebounded after it was safely recovered. By August, it had reached its peak. The discounts on various bonds were all above 75%, with the 9th Customs and the 9th Rehabilitation bonds nearly reaching 85%, and the interest rate was only around 0.7% per month. This led to selling by those with physical bonds. In addition, the United States raised silver prices, causing an outflow of silver, the foreign exchange rate rose, and credit tightened. The bond market gradually weakened, and the downward trend continued for several months. By December, the foreign exchange rate had soared and credit had become extremely tight, a rare occurrence in recent years. Banks urged the redemption of collateral loans and refused to conduct arbitrage transactions, cutting off the flow of capital to the bulls, which caused panic. Everyone sold off bonds, and the negotiable securities were crowded. The prices for the next month were inverted, and the predicament of the bulls was evident. The market was bleak, and it was difficult to recover. However, the average discount for the whole year was still better than that of the 22nd year by 12.656%, and the transaction volume was also very brisk. The comparative table of average discounts over the past three years, the comparative table of highest and lowest discounts, and the table of the proportion of delivered transaction amounts are listed below:

From observing the above table, the following points are noteworthy:

(1) Bond prices have been steadily rising over the past three years. The 22nd year was 9.13% higher than the 21st year, and the 23rd year was 12.65% higher than the 22nd year, and 21.786% higher than the 21st year. The bond with the largest price increase was the 18th Customs, with an increase of 24.405%, and the smallest increase was the 9th Customs, with as much as 18.885%. (See Table 1)

(2) The highest discounts over the years have all been for the 18th Customs, at 69.58% in the 21st year, 81.15% in the 22nd year, and 89.25% in the 23rd year (See Table 2), because the repayment period of this bond is approaching and there are fewer negotiable securities.

(3) The lowest discounts over the years have all been for the Reorganization 6% Bonds. At 26% in the 21st year, 34.20% in the 22nd year, and 45.70% in the 23rd year (See Table 2), because the bond only pays interest, and the redemption of principal by lottery will not be made until 1936.

(4) The largest difference in the 21st year was for the 18th Customs, at 25.18%. In the 22nd year, it was for the 9th Customs, at 29.64%. In the 23rd year, it was for the Disarmament Bonds, at 30.05%. (See Table 2)

(5) The smallest difference in the 21st year was for the Reorganization 6% Bonds, at 20.60%. In the 22nd year, it was for the Disarmament Bonds, at 25.45%. In the 23rd year, it was for the 23rd Customs, at only 8.58%. (See Table 2)

(6) The largest fluctuations in the bond market during the three years were in the 22nd year, at 27.129%, followed by the 23rd year, and the smallest in the 21st year. (See Table 2)

(7) The transaction volume was the highest in the 23rd year, 1,251,640,000 yuan more than the 22nd year, and as much as 3,869,885,000 yuan more than the 21st year. The total transaction volume of the 21st and 22nd years was not even equal to that of the 23rd year alone. The prosperity of the market can be seen. (See Table 3)

(8) The number of deliveries does not increase with the increase in the number of transactions, and the proportion decreases year by year. This is enough to prove that speculation is rampant and investment is small. Although the appearance seems firm, the underlying reality is weak. (See Table 5)

The high bond market is not so much a reflection of the prosperity of the financial sector, but rather a reflection of the unsoundness of our country's economy. The booming market is just a kind of abnormal state of reflected glory. Because inland cash is concentrated in Shanghai, and investment avenues are extremely narrow, everyone flocks to the buying and selling of bonds. When silver exports and credit suddenly tightened, physical bonds were sold. Therefore, the prosperity of bonds depends entirely on the overall economic shift. Over the past three years, the rise and fall of domestic prices have been less affected by political threats and more by economic control. When Rehe was lost and North China was in a serious state, bonds rose steadily. By the end of the 23rd year, foreign relations were becoming increasingly harmonious, the suppression of bandits had been successful, and the opinions of the central government and the southwest were gradually converging. The environment was good and people's hearts were stable, but the bond market was lifeless and weak, for no other reason than the fact that it was controlled by the economy.

Securities: Bond Market Fluctuates Like Waves Last Week 212

Last week (March 18th to 23rd) was the last week of March futures trading at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange. It happened to coincide with many events, and the market price fluctuated greatly. In Europe, there was Germany's military preparation. In this city, there was first the real estate developer's proposed 50 million yuan of circulating notes, followed by the exchange of 2,000 10,000-yuan notes for 1,000-yuan notes in the 22nd Customs, which suddenly increased the floating negotiable securities by 20 million. The 100 million financial bonds were about to be implemented, which would increase the capital of the Central Bank and the Bank of Communications, activate the market, and the 5 million syndicate loan was also about to be implemented. The market price was uncertain. Recently, due to the approaching settlement date, the price rise and fall depended only on the imbalance in the supply and demand of negotiable securities between the bulls and bears, and fluctuated from time to time, which was not the standard for rising and falling. On Monday and Tuesday, there were the above-mentioned factors, and there was a lot of short covering and bull exiting in the market. Big players also sold, and the market price dropped by a small half a yuan or so each day. On Wednesday, the rumor of circulating notes was invisibly eliminated, the short covering was made up, and the price rebounded unanimously by 3, 5, and 7 jiao or so. On Thursday, the 100 million financial bonds had been decided, and the market price fell again by 3, 5 jiao. On Friday, the short position rolled over and made up, and rebounded by 3, 4 jiao. On Saturday, there was still hope for foreign loans, and the 5 million syndicate loan was about to be established. Suddenly, there were big players buying in and covering short positions in the market, resulting in the abnormal situation of the near-term rising and the distant-term falling. In summary, the results of the market price for a week were quite chaotic, with mostly falling and less rising. Among them, there was still a phenomenon of near-high and far-low, the number was only between 5 fen, 1 jiao to 6, 7 jiao. The total transaction volume was 80,002,700 yuan. The results of the price increase and decrease are listed in the comparison table on the left (unit: yuan, transaction unit: 100 yuan).

American Cotton Has Bullish Clearing 215

Yesterday, the American cotton market was quite active. At the opening, both buyers and short sellers were very strong, so the market price did not fluctuate much from the previous day. Later, there was a lack of important buyers in the market, and at the same time, Wall Street was weak. Brokers cleared bullish positions, and foreign merchants sold, so the price gradually declined. When the price fell, the industry bought in slightly. The closing was flat. Spot prices fell by 10 points, and futures prices fell by 3 to 10 points. British cotton rose following American cotton. Speculators and the industry both purchased. Spot prices rose by 13 points, and futures prices rose by 13-14 points. Indian cotton was firm due to public buying. Textiles: Domestic "Huada Ne" Fabric Sells Exceptionally Well - Imports of Foreign Goods Decline Annually - 217

Yesterday, the trade in woolens remained brisk, with prices showing little fluctuation. However, the sales of Huada Ne and similar fabrics have decreased recently. Imports last year were more than half of what they were in 1933. Furthermore, colors and patterns have changed, and domestic products are well-made. Currently, the most popular items are plain Yuan Chang and gray, followed by mixed colors. The plaid and striped Huada Ne fabrics that were popular in the past are now outdated. Twill and dotted Ne fabrics also have very limited sales. Old-style mixed-color Ne fabrics with slight embellishments for shoe uppers are not often stocked by wool shops. Red, green, and iridescent Ne fabrics have long been eliminated. Therefore, this spring, only plain and mixed-color Ne fabrics have arrived, while other varieties are completely absent. Domestic products from the Da Long and Zhang Hua factories, such as Yuan Chang and gray plain Huada Ne fabrics, have good sales, which has slightly impacted foreign goods. Plain Huada Ne fabrics sell quickly as clothing materials for street-front shops, mostly sold to out-of-town customers and Western-style clothing shops. Prices are on average thirty to forty cents cheaper per yard than last year.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

More on Confucius's Revisiting the New World 218

— Donghong

In the previous edition of this publication, Mr. "Spring Rain's" article "Confucius's Revisiting the New World" was published. It was quite interesting to read, but the title is "Confucius's Revisiting the New World," while the tone of the article is not "revisiting the New World" at all, which makes it seem like the content doesn't match the title. Therefore, I am also borrowing Mr. Spring Rain's theme to express my humble opinion, which may be approved by Mr. Spring Rain.

Confucius was originally known for enjoying traveling. No matter who invited him, the old man always gladly accepted and never refused. Even the rebellious ministers Gongshan Furao sent someone to invite Confucius, and Confucius even wanted to go, but Zilu blocked him, so he ultimately did not go. Another rebel minister, Fufan, also once sent someone to invite Confucius, and Confucius also wanted to go, but Zilu blocked him again. Although Confucius grumbled a bit, he ultimately did not go. Moreover, in the countries Confucius visited, he only stopped by at the homes of a few acquaintances, such as Ju Boyu in the State of Wei and Sicheng Zhenzi in the State of Qi, who were his old patrons. No one ever built a "Confucius Mansion" to invite him to live there. Therefore, Confucius may not object to Japan's invitation this time.

Furthermore, Confucius often joked around with women. Nanzi, the wife of Duke Ling of Wei, sent someone to express her desire to see Confucius. Confucius met her, with the woman behind a curtain and Confucius outside the curtain, seeing each other through the curtain. Confucius entered, facing north and bowing, while the woman bowed twice from behind the curtain, with the jingling sounds of jade ornaments. Nanzi was originally a well-known socialite in the State of Wei. Therefore, Zilu, who was known for his simplicity, was very unhappy when he heard about this. Confucius hurriedly and solemnly declared, "Don't misunderstand. If I have any irregular thoughts, may Heaven abandon me. I can swear an oath in front of you." Last time, when the League of Nations investigation team visited Japan, Japan held a grand dance party, with powdered faces and green eyebrows everywhere, and the guests and hosts all enjoyed themselves. Assuming that Confucius goes to Japan this time, Japan will also treat him exceptionally well and hold a welcoming meeting. I think Confucius will also dance with his hands and feet, just like hearing the Shao music, and forget the taste of meat for three months.

Confucius was a connoisseur of treasures and an archaeologist. Therefore, he had a lot of research on antiques and art. Thus, Confucius once inquired about rituals from Lao Peng and learned to play the zither from Shi Xiang. Therefore, he liked to travel to various countries to increase his knowledge. Therefore, like Tang Sanzang going to the Western Buddhist Kingdom to obtain scriptures, he encountered many tribulations on the road, being rejected by Qi, expelled from Song and Wei, and trapped between Chen and Cai. However, Confucius still wanted to travel, planning to see Zhao Jianzi in the west. Upon hearing of the deaths of Dou Mingdu and Shun Hua in Awen, he lamented by the river, saying, "How beautiful is the water, so vast! It is fate that I cannot cross this river." Because he did not achieve his goal of going to Jin this time, he was very frustrated. Therefore, traveling to various countries was Confucius's favorite thing in his life. However, Confucius was not always welcomed wherever he went, and he was even driven away by people. Now that Confucius has been dead for a long time, there is only a wooden tablet. What does it matter where it goes? Therefore, no matter who wants to invite him, Confucius will definitely not object and will not cause any problems. Moreover, he himself said, "Qiu is a person of the east, west, south, and north." Therefore, he ran around his whole life and suffered a lot, but he did not regret it. Now, taking airplanes, trains, and ships to travel to various countries is truly getting what he wanted.

The Spring of Yushe Mountain 219

— Chunhui

It is spring, and life's laughter rises on Yushe Mountain. The sea makes a turn from Mazu Island, surrounding the Shantou Peninsula. Yushe Mountain stands opposite the city, rising up with the laughter of spring towards the city and the sea.

Ships of all sizes crowd densely in the bay. The spring sea only raises slight waves. The sun shines brightly on the water surface, and the shadows of the sails are dragged into large, black tails. The golden color of the sun reflects on the blue seawater

Page 20

reflecting onto the slopes of Yushe Mountain.

Many wooden boats cross the small sea journey daily, carrying guests between Shantou and Yushe Mountain. Steamships stir up waves, and the wooden boats sway, emitting sounds of oars.

From the peak of Yushe Mountain, the entire view of the sea is captured. The dense houses of Shantou City and the rows of giant buildings in front of the customs office are all revealed. The upper layers of the city are permeated with smoke, and the noise of the city can be heard across the sea. However, the fort at the mouth of the sea reveals its ugly and dark face, which is especially frightening in spring. Juxtaposed with the gentle face of the green mountain, it appears even more disharmonious.

Tender grass is green on the mountain, covering the paths. The red coffins in the Westerners' cemetery shine with a copper color in the spring. The cemetery is clean and full of wildflowers, and those who sleep there rest peacefully underground. Western-style houses are scattered on the mountain, with windows facing the sea. There are also small thatched cottages, whose humble appearance is covered by the warmth of spring.

The schools and dormitories on the mountainside often broadcast laughter. The sounds of balls are noisy on the sports fields, and young people display the vitality of youth.

In the morning and evening, foreigners often stroll the mountain paths with slender-waisted women. On sunny afternoons, there are also tourists coming across the sea, their neat Western clothes often matching silk cheongsams. In the very early morning, students run around in the mountains with nimble bodies.

Whenever small foreign warships are anchored in the sea, groups of two or three sailors, dressed in sailor uniforms, drill in the mountains. Occasionally, some fishermen step heavily in the mountains with firm strides.

Consuls tread with the affected gait of foreign gentlemen, while young female students, in simple tops and pleated skirts, walk with natural and lively lightness.

Looking behind from Yushe Mountain, the vast plain reveals green fields. Many small villages are sparsely scattered among the fields, with small houses gathered in piles. Groves of trees surround the villages, creating dividing lines with the boundless green fields.

Rivers flow smoothly on both sides of Yushe Mountain. From the mountain, the red color of the water looks like a red cloth belt. Mazu Island tightens its narrow mouth, and the sea water looks like a large pond. During high and low tides, the surging sea tide is as majestic as soldiers charging into battle.

Moonlit nights on Yushe Mountain in spring are even more exceptionally gentle and beautiful. The noise of the city is separated by a thin sea, and here it is as quiet as nature taking a nap. Moonlight shines all over the mountains, and poetic sentiments flow on every stone and every piece of soil. The residents of Yushe Mountain sleep in the moonlight, and it is easier to have sweet dreams than in other places.

In spring, the mountains laugh, and the sea laughs; the red flowers are shy, and the green grass is charming;… people wake up from the cold of winter and smile at the sea, the mountains, the flowers, and the grass.

The whole spring of Yushe Mountain is filled with laughter!

Spring Field Scenery 220

— Qin Jian

(The warm March sun slowly, like a divine miracle, drifts down from page to page of the calendar. People seem to have a little awakening from their comatose or decadent desires: we remember: it's spring.)

It is spring. The depressed world of humanity is forever greedily seeking the next new stimulus in its wild abandon. Therefore, when the red and the smiles have lost their stimulation in their cloying familiarity, everyone shouts frantically: It is spring, let's go to the fields, let's go to the fields!

(-Let's go to the countryside, let's go to the countryside to see the spring!

-Isn't it? Cities are damned, there is no spring or autumn in the cities – stupid cow!

-Daddy, darling, I'm so glad, I haven't seen the simplicity of the country people in this green life. I think it must be very lovely - I've seen those poetic descriptions in Hardy's rural novels.

-Yes, darling.)

Following the drift of the gentlemen's cigars, the express train clenches the tracks and rushes forward: red flowers and green weeds are already the spring countryside!

Is it true that the fields are as beautiful as poetry, even as the metropolis presents a shaky year?

People, following the warming of the climate, gradually increase; scattered in clusters in all directions, listening to the cunning tongue of the wild lark, listening to the flow of the stream, listening to the sound of a clock in the dusk, and finally, they also listen to the heavy sigh that fills the fields.

Since the beginning of spring, even the grain shops in the small towns have closed their doors one after another. The local bullies who usually strut on the streets, with their clothes unbuttoned, and who flirt with women, have fallen into even more dire straits, because the tea houses have closed and the gambling stalls have long been empty - people have become empty shells, what is there to gamble on?

And, on the other hand, following the decline of the townships, the people in the fields also pour out their melancholy of the troubled times into the open fields: panic, hunger; and the sighs of the elderly and the resentment of the young woven into the transition of the times.

The lack of something to fill the stomach is the most terrible thing. Last year was a drought, what is there to be happy about this spring? At home: the young lads have all drifted away, not knowing where they have gone. Around the Qingming Festival, the cemeteries everywhere are still deserted, you don't see the flying paper ash, and you don't hear the moving cries of the young widows. In this year, the dead are much happier than the living. Besides: even people can't take care of themselves, how can they take care of the dead ghosts, ha!

A kind of melancholy tune crosses the fields; nature stubbornly follows the discipline of the seasons: it is spring, and it still hangs up the flower buds and the tiny grass leaves: but when people are worried about the next meal, who still yearns for those worthless flowers and grasses?

But, finally, there are some people who come from a strange place - from the metropolis, who, in their smiling faces and gold-rimmed glasses, appreciate those flowers and grasses that are neglected by others. Spring is the golden age of Mother Nature, spring lives in the suburbs!

(Red butterflies, yellow butterflies, fly away like fallen flowers, swirling in the fields is a kind of indelible brown melancholy, like dark clouds before a big thunderstorm, which makes people suffocate!)

Three days, a week, someone in the first-class carriage of the spring tour train is thinking:

"The spring in the fields is not as lovely as the poets describe."

Shicha Lake 221

— Juefu

I spent a large portion of my days by this lakeside with a strong earthy smell, and I buried all my refreshing mornings and dim dusks in its embrace. I am very clear about what its true face is like.

There, no matter which refreshing day it is, there will always be small birds jumping and singing on the willows, white pigeons circling in the sky, occasionally emitting哇哇... whistle sounds; old men carrying bird cages, pacing back and forth under the willow shade, strong men carrying baskets and nets, netting fish in the small river by the lake, farmers and farm women wearing straw hats and carrying hoes, working hard in the fields... people who are placed here will forget that they are living in a metropolis with one or two million people. When the evening mist gradually descends, the crows returning from their tired travels, fill the sky with red clouds, hovering and clamoring, and teams of gray and white ducks also flap their wings, jump into the clear water, and wander around aimlessly. The blood-red sunset hangs obliquely on the city walls that resemble mountains, and the weeping willows far and near are shrouded in a thin layer of mist; looking through the light mist to the east, standing there is a majestic ancient drum tower and bell tower, covered with a layer of light-colored sunset. At this time, what unfolds before your eyes is not just a wonderful natural group painting?

It was in the severe cold of winter, right? The lotus flowers that rippled on the water surface could not withstand the blowing of the biting cold wind and had long since withered and sunk. At this time, what was spread in the lake was a piece of bright, thick ice bed. The swimming bed has become the only entertainment place for a group of poor families: the children, using their homemade ice skates, are strolling on it; the strong men, pull down their ice boats, (the so-called ice boats are just large tables with two iron bars embedded underneath) carrying guests back and forth on it. For families who cannot afford a pair of ice skates, if they also want to enjoy the taste of skating on the ice, spending four or five copper coins to take an ice boat ride is considered a reward. Once spring arrives, when the ice bed gradually melts into clear water, the strong winds unique to the north blow day and night, and the bare willow stalks occasionally make呼呼呼... cries, and the sea water is like a vast ocean, one wave after another, rolling towards the other shore. Standing on the mound by the lake, looking up at the lake, looking at the willow branches, it will teach people to unconsciously feel like they are about to become immortals. When the spring light is old, the willow leaves gradually become lush green on the branches, and the lotus flowers in the lake also stretch out of the water, swaying in the wind. When the scorching summer sun comes, listening to the clear birdsong, smelling the fragrant lotus fragrance, the clear scenery of so-called warm sun, fish leaping, quiet water surface, light wind, birds singing, cool shade of trees, is now vividly appearing before our eyes. By the time summer goes and autumn comes, the lush green weeping willows are covered with a layer of light yellow outerwear, and the lotus flowers in the lake have long since withered, and the basin-like leaves are also showing signs of withering. If it is a rest day, when a person walks alone on the riverbank with an umbrella, or walks into the tea house by the lake, leaning on the railing to drink alone, then the secluded pleasure of leaving the residual lotus to listen to the rain is now being appreciated.

A place with such a strong rural flavor will never be forgotten in the minds of us country people who are used to living in the city!

Nostalgia 222

— Yangyang

Memories are like a heavy fog; in loneliness, my mind falls into contemplation again!

Although the surface of the city is prosperous, the state of mind of a wanderer is like a piece of ice; there is never a time when it is warm. Even if there is, it is only temporary.

The spring light seems to be even more brilliant in a few drizzles! The beautiful season makes every heart sink even more into old sweetness.

The taste of first love is like honey. The ancient mountain peaks of Nanhua are the place I cherish the most! Once the plum blossoms withered, people took off their heavy furs and put on light spring clothes.

When the sunset reflects on the decadent branches of the plum blossoms, the sound of the bells of Cangshan reverberates with medieval fantasies. Everyone carries leather-bound books and comes out of the old Western-style buildings; strolling on the tidy mountain road.

The broken shadows of sunlight are filtered through the banyan trees on both sides, stepping on the monument commemorating the restoration; watching a round of rising sun gradually sink westward on the other side of Yushan.

At the second sound of the bell, it floats over from the bell tower again. At this time, a superior-level guard climbs up from the iron ladder. A person with a haggard expression then comes down.

Going down the stone steps of the mountain road, you can see the Minjiang River like a silver chain in the middle. In the rapids of the Jiangnan Bridge, white waves splash everywhere. Walking across the Jiangnan Bridge to an island surrounded by water, this is our home!

On this island, we spent years and years of time flowing like mercury. Watching the prosperity of this small island, this small island also declined with the years of war. At the mouth of the Minjiang River, the imperialist shallow-water ships also devoured the entire prosperity!

It was in a period of great turmoil that I left this mountain valley and water village; it now seems like a long century has passed.

But the news that came back is that this island is even more mired in the vortex of depression. This solid fossil will one day be broken by the big waves!

In my heart, infinite melancholy has increased again.

Let people criticize her for spinning hemp during the day and weaving yarn at night. Let them call her disheveled and barefoot. It is just that heaven does not grant her wishes. She is like a lone goose falling on the sand. How can she not resent her parents?

Shen Bao Local Supplement, Movie Special

A Study of the Names of the Latest Forty Love Films 245

— Boning

Every Saturday, when I breathe a sigh of relief after leaving the office, the first thing I do is ask people, "Where are you going to see a movie this afternoon?" Especially the author, I like to ask an extra question: "Why are you going there? Why are you going to see that film?" After asking many, many times, asking countless people, their answers can be summarized into only three sentences: "I know that film is good." "The location there is more suitable." "That film seems to be very good."

Regarding the first type, it is due to the high value of the film itself and the merit of film reviews. Because before watching a movie, most people first browse the film reviews of the day, or ask people who have seen it, and then go to see it after knowing the quality of the film. The second type is about the film itself, the price, equipment, and location, which are naturally more attractive. Only the third type of people rely entirely on intuition. They have no preference for theaters, have not read film reviews, and no one has told them that the film is good. They casually see the name of a film in the newspaper, on the roadside advertisement, or even when walking past the theater entrance, and if it appeals to them, they go straight in. Whose merit is this? It's the "film title." The name of a film, like an article or a book, has great value and great magic, so it is also the easiest to move people.

For this reason, the author collected many film titles from February to the present and analyzed and studied them. Among them, the names of domestic films are generally better, with fewer flaws. This is because domestic productions are not easy, and choosing a name is naturally cautious and not taken lightly. As for foreign films, they are much worse. Therefore, this article only focuses on foreign films, but among foreign films, comedies, war films, detective films, and silent films, although there are some materials, are ultimately few in number and not enough for analysis, so it only adopts a portion of "love films." Now, the results of the research are briefly described.

Too much repetition of words and phrases. A total of forty love films were collected this time (film titles omitted). The author analyzed the individual characters among them and found that the most frequent character was "情" (love), appearing thirteen times, accounting for 32.5%; "春" (spring) appeared five times, accounting for 12.5%; "女" (woman) and "風" (wind) each accounted for nine times. Analyzing individual phrases, "春風" (spring breeze) was found twice, and "情史" (love history) was also found twice. If we further analyze similar phrases, then we already have "春風" (spring breeze) and also "春光" (spring light), "春色" (spring color), "春心" (spring heart). We already have "情深" (deep love) and also "多情" (affectionate), "情奔" (love run), "情侶" (lovers), "情種" (love seed), "懺情" (confession of love)...etc. Whether from a psychological perspective or an advertising perspective, such "repetition" is a huge flaw. For example, when "dating," if you keep saying "I love you, I love you, I love you" to your lover, without any variation, will the other party be moved? Will they sympathize with you?

Too many vague phrases... Among these forty films, there is a large pile of vague phrases, such as: "媚月" (charming moon), "春風" (spring breeze), "憐香" (pitying fragrance), "竊玉" (stealing jade), "靈犀" (telepathy)...etc. If you were to stare at a wall with these words like "憐香," "竊玉," "靈犀" arranged side by side, and were asked to choose one, which would you choose and which would you reject? Then how can this large pile attract the audience to succeed?

Too many rigid numbers of characters... Among the forty films this time, thirty-one have names with four characters. This accounts for almost 80% of the total. If we walk into the City God Temple or the Guan Emperor Temple and look up at the four-character plaques arranged there, what do we feel? Don't we just feel that they are "similar," "almost the same," and have no impression other than the temple door? Then what do the movie audiences feel about these neatly arranged film titles?

Because of the above three shortcomings, we often feel that foreign films, especially love films, are all: "irrelevant," all "cold," without passionate feelings, without a fire-like attraction, leading us to appreciate them. This is so unfortunate!

Film Review

Review of "The Gay Bride" 246

— Hualun

"The Gay Bride" - Showing in Nanjing

The appearance and activity of private thugs and bullies in today's society is more rampant than in the past. This phenomenon also reflects the inherent contradictions, anxieties, and festering knots within this society. Look, especially in so-called modern civilized metropolises, or political centers, commercial centers, the actions of these tycoons among private thugs and bullies are revealed daily in newspapers, such as creating disturbances, open killings and assassinations, and revenge. Last night, they were fighting each other over jealousy or disagreements, but today, because there are benefits to be gained or power to borrow, they conspire and cooperate as if nothing had happened. On the surface, they are associating with the powerful and participating in good deeds to gain political and social status; secretly, they are engaging in all sorts of illegal and criminal activities.

There are also women who are unscrupulous and only care about profit. Tonight, they are in the arms of their lovers, and tomorrow they will accept expensive ornaments from the hands of the people who killed their lovers. The day after tomorrow, they will repeat this set of tricks as usual. Therefore, some people say that gangsters and prostitutes are the elements and characteristics of capitalist society. If someone were to thoroughly and deeply describe the lives of these gangsters and bullies, they could write a work even greater than Zola's series or Tolstoy's "War and Peace."

This film "The Gay Bride" depicts the lives of gangsters. Of course, it only uses the trivial matters of a few private thugs in a certain region of the Atlantic as its subject matter, and the author cannot fully express himself, so the achievement is limited.

It starts with the entanglement between the gangster Su Shi and the actress Man Lan. From the revenge of the enemy party on the day of their marriage, the coveting of the bride by his trusted followers Ding Gan and Mi Gai, and the bodyguard's (little errand boy) resistance and advice, it introduces five or six character lines. It writes about the mutual deception and mutual killing between men and women, money and flesh, and the decadent lives of money and flesh. Naturally, these realities related to the current social system are not vividly captured by the author through his narrow and shallow understanding. It is only a part of the relationships between them - the gangsters. It neglects their role in helping those above them and their mission of oppressing those below them in the current society. Moreover, it embellishes reality and uses ridiculous moralizing, such as portraying the gangster's loyal bodyguard (little errand boy) as so loyal and chivalrous, making people forget that he is an accomplice who protects whom? And arousing goodwill towards the gangster. As well as using the actress, the female gangster who played with so many gangsters, to realize that she took the tens of thousands of family property that she had repeatedly tricked out with her body and distributed it on the street as a great philanthropist to help the poor. As for the fact that when Su Shi and his wife went on their honeymoon to Europe, many countries refused them entry, this is also a deceiving lie. In fact, gangsters like Su Shi in the play who traffic in alcohol and play with women, as long as they do not have ambitions to rebel, as portrayed in the play, except for some competition among peers for fame, power, and women, they have not committed any heinous crimes, and the authorities would not refuse them entry.

The director Jack Conway has achieved commendable results in "The Gay Bride". He accurately grasps the atmosphere of the gangster's life throughout the play and clearly portrays the five or six character lines. In particular, the personality of the little errand boy, every scene, everyone's coming and going, is given a moving and profound sense of inspiration by this atmosphere and character. In comparison, the results in several large scenes are not as great as many small places with cleverness. Originally, it was a rough, lively, and superficial script, but it achieved delicate and meticulous effects.

Among the actors, Chester Morris, who played the little errand boy, left the deepest impression.

Joan Parker playing the goddess of nature in "She Creature" - Showing in Nanjing

The Earth-Shattering "She Creature" 247

— Yunshui

Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer spent a year producing this rare and magnificent beast film, hailed as one of the best in twenty years. The great director Van Dyke Ming calls the film this year's most successful and stimulating beast drama, and the famous American novelist Zane Grey also praised it highly, recommending it as a unique work in ten years. (Grey is a master of Western novels, and many of his works have been successfully adapted for the screen, especially Trader Horn). On the star list, the charming and lively seventeen-year-old girl Joan Parker takes the lead, while the backbone of the play is two beast stars, one is a strong deer, who plays Malibu in "She Creature", and the other is a mountain lion Puma (American lion species) whose name is Gando.

Obviously, the law of the jungle in the forest has always been regarded as the iron law of evolution. But after all, all things are endowed with compassion, and all acts of predation and killing ultimately stem from some kind of impulse. Probably, birds flying in the sky, beasts walking on land, scales living in water, and insects hiding in mud can never escape the two major circles of "food" and "sex." What is called love is the root of life, and life depends on desire. Regardless of the type of animal, they are equally endowed with the function of survival, such as claws, fangs, stings, and venom, skin armor, feathers, and hair, which are innate protective tools. Then, a question arises here: do humans' intellect - the tool for protecting the survival of the race - and compassion, also have this special function? Or do they merely kill to survive, and survive to kill? That's right, "She Creature," which will be released in Nanjing soon, can give us a very satisfactory answer.

Jottings "Wife's Lover" 248

— Guocheng

RKO's new film "Wife's Lover" (Head Coat and Glove) is a story about a mysterious murder that occurs with both romantic and suspicious elements.

The original name of "Wife's Lover" should be translated directly as "Hat, Coat, and Glove." Therefore, we can certainly know how important these three things are in this film. If you want to use the simplest method to explain the relationship between these three things, it is like this: when this mysterious murder happened to a girl, people found her body in her lover's room, and at this time, a woman's hat and a man's coat and a glove were found in the room, and these things were used as clues in the case.

At least, this is a very tragic and moving film. Every scene in the play is filled with a tense atmosphere. The actors Rich do Cordeg and Barbara Robbins are both working hard in this film. The director's technique is also very easy. When the film was released in New York, it received praise from more than a dozen newspapers such as the "New York Daily News" and the "New York Evening Post."

Movie Novel

The Hatred of India's Subjugation (Clive of India) (9) 249

— Maode

When Clive arrived in India, he observed the overall situation and felt that the only way to rebuild a solid foundation for his country's merchants was to use Mir Jafar. Siraj ud-Daulah was a cruel and despicable person. Mir Jafar was relatively easy to manipulate. He was Siraj ud-Daulah's uncle and now led Siraj ud-Daulah's army. Although he was in opposition to the British, if he could be moved by profit and made to turn against his own side, then the British could win without a fight. Therefore, Clive wanted to collude with Mir Jafar and make a secret agreement with him: if he could turn against his own side, Britain would do everything in its power to guarantee that he would become the King of India, and the reward that Britain sought was merely the ability to continue free trade.

Clive did nothing without consulting Margaret. He told Margaret, and she wondered, "This seems to go beyond your military scope." Clive proudly said, "We must now use political tactics. Our current work is the creation of an empire!" So he went to secretly negotiate with Mir Jafar. Mir Jafar actually expressed acceptance of his idea, but he insisted that the British Admiral Watson, stationed in India, sign the agreement before Mir Jafar would agree. Therefore, Clive had to consult with Watson again.

Admiral Watson was an old, corpulent British naval veteran. At first, when he heard that Mir Jafar had promised that if he signed the secret agreement, he would pay him 40,000 pounds in cash every year, he couldn't help but be moved. He held the pen in his hand and carefully read the clauses of the secret agreement on the table, looking for whether the gift of 40,000 pounds a year was clearly stated. He was about to sign, but suddenly became frightened and withdrew his hand. He thought to himself, what if this matter doesn't succeed... what if they lose the war... the secret agreement falls into the hands of others... with his name on it... what would happen then? He was a prudent person. He couldn't swallow this piece of fat. So he repeatedly shook his head and said, "No, no. My conscience does not allow this thing."

Clive said, "If you don't sign, the whole plan will fail, and the empire will not be established." But once Watson had doubts, no matter how Clive explained, he could no longer move his heart. What he feared was Mir Jafar's reversal, but he kept saying that his conscience did not allow him to do such a thing.

Watson left, and Edmund ran in. He saw the disappointed look on Clive's face and said, "Then everything is over. Mir Jafar will definitely use all his strength against us." Clive frowned, suddenly laughed loudly and said, "This matter must be carried out according to the original plan, it cannot be a failure." Edmund was in shock, Clive had already picked up the pen and signed the name of "Charles Watson" on the secret agreement.

Edmund exclaimed in horror, "He will know." Clive said, "If the war is won, Watson will be the first to rush to recognize this secret agreement. Take this to Mir Jafar!" After he finished speaking, his body collapsed in the chair, and he held his head where the old wound had flared up again. Edmund shouted beside him, "Robert!" Clive also ordered, "Pass the order down. March tomorrow morning!"

By the next morning, Clive was wearing his military uniform, standing by the window, listening to the bugle calls outside, already prepared to depart. Infantry squads marched past one after another. Many elephants and camels carrying military supplies, guns, cannons, and food also set off. This was much more organized than the "madman team" a few years ago, but it was still far inferior to Siraj ud-Daulah's army. (To be continued)
